   1 | # Alianza Residencial — Instrucciones de instalación de escritorio
   2 | 
   3 | ## ¿Qué se entrega en este paquete?
   4 | 
   5 | | Archivo | Acción |
   6 | |---------|--------|
   7 | | `launcher.py` | **Reemplaza** `Run.py` como punto de entrada principal |
   8 | | `main.js` | **Reemplaza** `app/static/js/main.js` |
   9 | | `app_main.py` | **Reemplaza** `app/main.py` (renombrar a `main.py`) |
  10 | | `auth_service.py` | **Reemplaza** `app/services/auth_service.py` |
  11 | | `build.bat` | Nuevo — genera el `.exe` instalable |
  12 | 
  13 | ---
  14 | 
  15 | ## Paso 1 — Copiar archivos
  16 | 
  17 | ```
  18 | launcher.py          →  C:\alianza_backend\launcher.py
  19 | main.js              →  C:\alianza_backend\app\static\js\main.js
  20 | app_main.py          →  C:\alianza_backend\app\main.py   (renombrar)
  21 | auth_service.py      →  C:\alianza_backend\app\services\auth_service.py
  22 | build.bat            →  C:\alianza_backend\build.bat
  23 | ```
  24 | 
  25 | ---
  26 | 
  27 | ## Paso 2 — Probar localmente
  28 | 
  29 | ```bash
  30 | cd C:\alianza_backend
  31 | python launcher.py
  32 | ```
  33 | 
  34 | Verás una ventana con:
  35 | - Indicador LED rojo/verde del servidor
  36 | - Log de actividad en tiempo real
  37 | - Botón **Iniciar Sistema** → arranca FastAPI + abre el navegador
  38 | - Botón **Abrir navegador** → abre `http://localhost:8000`
  39 | - Botón **Detener** → para el servidor limpiamente
  40 | 
  41 | Al iniciar, el sistema:
  42 | 1. Verifica dependencias (`pip install -r requirements.txt`)
  43 | 2. Crea las carpetas `database/`, `logs/`, `invoices/`
  44 | 3. Arranca uvicorn en el puerto 8000
  45 | 4. Espera que el servidor responda
  46 | 5. Abre el navegador automáticamente en el login
  47 | 
  48 | ---
  49 | 
  50 | ## Paso 3 — Qué cambió en el código
  51 | 
  52 | ### `main.js` (frontend)
  53 | - Añadido objeto `Auth` — guarda/lee el token JWT en localStorage
  54 | - `apiRequest()` ahora envía `Authorization: Bearer <token>` en cada petición
  55 | - Si el servidor responde 401, limpia la sesión y redirige al login
  56 | - `renderHeader()` muestra el nombre del usuario y botón de logout
  57 | - Nueva función `logout()` — limpia localStorage y va al login
  58 | 
  59 | ### `app/main.py`
  60 | - Al arrancar, llama `create_default_admin()` — crea usuario admin si no existe
  61 | - Las rutas de API están bajo `/api` (coincide con el frontend)
  62 | 
  63 | ### `app/services/auth_service.py`
  64 | - Nueva función `create_default_admin(db)` — crea admin desde variables del `.env`
  65 | 
  66 | ---
  67 | 
  68 | ## Paso 4 — Generar el .exe (opcional, para distribuir)
  69 | 
  70 | Instalar PyInstaller:
  71 | ```bash
  72 | pip install pyinstaller
  73 | ```
  74 | 
  75 | Ejecutar el build:
  76 | ```
  77 | Doble clic en build.bat
  78 | ```
  79 | 
  80 | El resultado estará en:
  81 | ```
  82 | dist\AlianzaResidencial\AlianzaResidencial.exe
  83 | ```
  84 | 
  85 | Para distribuir al cliente: comprimir toda la carpeta `dist\AlianzaResidencial\` en un ZIP.
  86 | 
  87 | > **Nota:** El `.exe` incluye Python y todas las dependencias. El cliente solo necesita
  88 | > hacer doble clic — no necesita instalar Python.
  89 | 
  90 | ---
  91 | 
  92 | ## Credenciales por defecto
  93 | 
  94 | - **Usuario:** admin  
  95 | - **Contraseña:** Admin123
  96 | 
  97 | Se pueden cambiar en el archivo `.env`:
  98 | ```
  99 | DEFAULT_ADMIN_USER=admin
 100 | DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASS=Admin123
 101 | ```
 102 | 
 103 | ---
 104 | 
 105 | ## Próximos pasos sugeridos
 106 | 
 107 | 1. Generar el `.exe` y probarlo en una PC limpia (sin Python instalado)
 108 | 2. Crear un ícono `assets/icon.ico` para personalizar el launcher
 109 | 3. Agregar un instalador con Inno Setup (crea el típico "siguiente → siguiente → instalar")
 110 | 4. Cuando estés listo para agregar más funciones, continuar con el desarrollo normal
 111 |

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: build.bat
TIPO: BAT
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\build.bat
================================================================================

   1 | @echo off
   2 | REM ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   3 | REM  ALIANZA RESIDENCIAL — Build .exe para Windows
   4 | REM  Resultado: dist\AlianzaResidencial\AlianzaResidencial.exe
   5 | REM  Requiere Python + pip install pyinstaller
   6 | REM ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   7 | 
   8 | echo.
   9 | echo  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════╗
  10 | echo  ║  ALIANZA RESIDENCIAL — Generando .exe   ║
  11 | echo  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════╝
  12 | echo.
  13 | 
  14 | pip show pyinstaller >nul 2>&1
  15 | if errorlevel 1 (
  16 |     echo  Instalando PyInstaller...
  17 |     pip install pyinstaller
  18 | )
  19 | 
  20 | if exist dist\AlianzaResidencial rmdir /s /q dist\AlianzaResidencial
  21 | if exist build rmdir /s /q build
  22 | if exist AlianzaResidencial.spec del AlianzaResidencial.spec
  23 | 
  24 | echo  Compilando... (puede tardar 2-5 minutos)
  25 | echo.
  26 | 
  27 | pyinstaller ^
  28 |   --name "AlianzaResidencial" ^
  29 |   --onedir ^
  30 |   --windowed ^
  31 |   --add-data "app;app" ^
  32 |   --add-data ".env;." ^
  33 |   --add-data "requirements.txt;." ^
  34 |   --hidden-import "uvicorn.logging" ^
  35 |   --hidden-import "uvicorn.loops.auto" ^
  36 |   --hidden-import "uvicorn.protocols.http.auto" ^
  37 |   --hidden-import "uvicorn.protocols.websockets.auto" ^
  38 |   --hidden-import "uvicorn.lifespan.on" ^
  39 |   --hidden-import "passlib.handlers.bcrypt" ^
  40 |   --hidden-import "jose" ^
  41 |   --hidden-import "sqlalchemy.dialects.sqlite" ^
  42 |   --hidden-import "pydantic_settings" ^
  43 |   --collect-all "fastapi" ^
  44 |   --collect-all "sqlalchemy" ^
  45 |   --noconfirm ^
  46 |   launcher.py
  47 | 
  48 | if errorlevel 1 (
  49 |     echo.
  50 |     echo  ERROR durante la compilacion.
  51 |     pause & exit /b 1
  52 | )
  53 | 
  54 | echo.
  55 | echo  Copiando archivos de datos...
  56 | copy .env "dist\AlianzaResidencial\" >nul 2>&1
  57 | mkdir "dist\AlianzaResidencial\database" 2>nul
  58 | mkdir "dist\AlianzaResidencial\logs"     2>nul
  59 | mkdir "dist\AlianzaResidencial\invoices" 2>nul
  60 | 
  61 | echo.
  62 | echo  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════╗
  63 | echo  ║  Build completado exitosamente  ✓        ║
  64 | echo  ║                                          ║
  65 | echo  ║  Carpeta: dist\AlianzaResidencial\       ║
  66 | echo  ║  Archivo: AlianzaResidencial.exe         ║
  67 | echo  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════╝
  68 | echo.
  69 | echo  Para distribuir: comprime dist\AlianzaResidencial\
  70 | echo.
  71 | pause
  72 |

   1 | """
   2 | Alianza Residencial — Launcher de escritorio
   3 | Ventana nativa con tkinter que controla el servidor FastAPI.
   4 | Ejecutar: python launcher.py
   5 | """
   6 | 
   7 | import tkinter as tk
   8 | from tkinter import messagebox
   9 | import threading
  10 | import subprocess
  11 | import sys
  12 | import os
  13 | import time
  14 | import webbrowser
  15 | import socket
  16 | from pathlib import Path
  17 | 
  18 | # ─── Configuración ──────────────────────────
  19 | APP_NAME = "Alianza Residencial"
  20 | APP_URL  = "http://localhost:8000"
  21 | PORT     = 8000
  22 | 
  23 | C_BG      = "#f0f2f5"
  24 | C_DARK    = "#0a2c5e"
  25 | C_DARK2   = "#1e4a8c"
  26 | C_WHITE   = "#ffffff"
  27 | C_SUCCESS = "#10b981"
  28 | C_DANGER  = "#ef4444"
  29 | C_MUTED   = "#5a6a7e"
  30 | C_BORDER  = "#e6e9f0"
  31 | C_TEXT    = "#1a2639"
  32 | 
  33 | 
  34 | def port_free(port: int) -> bool:
  35 |     with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as s:
  36 |         return s.connect_ex(("localhost", port)) != 0
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def wait_server(port: int, timeout=30) -> bool:
  40 |     t = time.time()
  41 |     while time.time() - t < timeout:
  42 |         if not port_free(port):
  43 |             return True
  44 |         time.sleep(0.4)
  45 |     return False
  46 | 
  47 | 
  48 | def get_python() -> str:
  49 |     for p in [Path("venv/Scripts/python.exe"), Path("venv/bin/python")]:
  50 |         if p.exists():
  51 |             return str(p)
  52 |     return sys.executable
  53 | 
  54 | 
  55 | # ─── Ventana principal ───────────────────────
  56 | class Launcher:
  57 |     def __init__(self):
  58 |         self.proc    = None
  59 |         self.running = False
  60 | 
  61 |         self.root = tk.Tk()
  62 |         self.root.title("Alianza Residencial — Launcher")
  63 |         self.root.resizable(False, False)
  64 |         self.root.configure(bg=C_BG)
  65 | 
  66 |         w, h = 460, 550
  67 |         sw = self.root.winfo_screenwidth()
  68 |         sh = self.root.winfo_screenheight()
  69 |         self.root.geometry(f"{w}x{h}+{(sw-w)//2}+{(sh-h)//2}")
  70 | 
  71 |         for ico in [Path("assets/icon.ico"), Path("app/static/favicon.ico")]:
  72 |             if ico.exists():
  73 |                 try: self.root.iconbitmap(str(ico))
  74 |                 except: pass
  75 |                 break
  76 | 
  77 |         self._ui()
  78 |         self.root.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", self._close)
  79 | 
  80 |     # ── Construir UI ─────────────────────────
  81 |     def _ui(self):
  82 |         # Header azul
  83 |         hdr = tk.Frame(self.root, bg=C_DARK, height=112)
  84 |         hdr.pack(fill="x")
  85 |         hdr.pack_propagate(False)
  86 | 
  87 |         logo = tk.Frame(hdr, bg=C_DARK2, width=52, height=52)
  88 |         logo.place(x=22, y=30)
  89 |         logo.pack_propagate(False)
  90 |         tk.Label(logo, text="AR", bg=C_DARK2, fg=C_WHITE,
  91 |                  font=("Segoe UI", 17, "bold")).place(relx=.5, rely=.5, anchor="center")
  92 | 
  93 |         tk.Label(hdr, text="ALIANZA RESIDENCIAL", bg=C_DARK, fg=C_WHITE,
  94 |                  font=("Segoe UI", 13, "bold")).place(x=90, y=30)
  95 |         tk.Label(hdr, text="Sistema de Administración de Propiedades",
  96 |                  bg=C_DARK, fg="#7aa8d4", font=("Segoe UI", 9)).place(x=90, y=57)
  97 |         tk.Label(hdr, text="v1.0  ·  Base de datos local",
  98 |                  bg=C_DARK, fg="#3a5e82", font=("Segoe UI", 8)).place(x=90, y=79)
  99 | 
 100 |         # Body
 101 |         body = tk.Frame(self.root, bg=C_BG)
 102 |         body.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=22, pady=18)
 103 | 
 104 |         # — Tarjeta de estado —
 105 |         sc = tk.Frame(body, bg=C_WHITE, highlightbackground=C_BORDER, highlightthickness=1)
 106 |         sc.pack(fill="x", pady=(0, 12))
 107 | 
 108 |         tk.Label(sc, text="ESTADO DEL SERVIDOR", bg=C_WHITE, fg=C_MUTED,
 109 |                  font=("Segoe UI", 7, "bold")).pack(anchor="w", padx=14, pady=(11, 3))
 110 | 
 111 |         srow = tk.Frame(sc, bg=C_WHITE)
 112 |         srow.pack(fill="x", padx=14, pady=(0, 4))
 113 | 
 114 |         self.led_cv = tk.Canvas(srow, width=14, height=14, bg=C_WHITE, highlightthickness=0)
 115 |         self.led_cv.pack(side="left")
 116 |         self.led = self.led_cv.create_oval(2, 2, 12, 12, fill=C_DANGER, outline="")
 117 | 
 118 |         self.lbl_status = tk.Label(srow, text="Detenido", bg=C_WHITE, fg=C_DANGER,
 119 |                                    font=("Segoe UI", 11, "bold"))
 120 |         self.lbl_status.pack(side="left", padx=(8, 0))
 121 |

 125 |         self.lbl_url.bind("<Button-1>", lambda _: self._open())

 178 |     # ── Logging ──────────────────────────────
 179 |     def _log(self, msg: str, level="info"):
 180 |         ts  = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
 181 |         sym = {"ok": "✓", "err": "✕", "warn": "⚠"}.get(level, "·")
 182 |         self.log.configure(state="normal")
 183 |         self.log.insert("end", f"[{ts}] {sym} {msg}\n", level if level != "info" else "")
 184 |         self.log.see("end")
 185 |         self.log.configure(state="disabled")
 186 | 
 187 |     # ── Estado UI ────────────────────────────
 188 |     def _set_running(self, on: bool):
 189 |         if on:
 190 |             self.led_cv.itemconfig(self.led, fill=C_SUCCESS)
 191 |             self.lbl_status.config(text="Activo", fg=C_SUCCESS)
 192 |             self.lbl_url.config(text=f"↗  {APP_URL}   (clic para abrir)")
 193 |             self.btn_start.config(state="disabled", bg="#94a3b8", text="▶   Activo")
 194 |             self.btn_open.config(state="normal")
 195 |             self.btn_stop.config(state="normal")
 196 |         else:
 197 |             self.led_cv.itemconfig(self.led, fill=C_DANGER)
 198 |             self.lbl_status.config(text="Detenido", fg=C_DANGER)
 199 |             self.lbl_url.config(text="")
 200 |             self.btn_start.config(state="normal", bg=C_DARK, text="▶   Iniciar Sistema")
 201 |             self.btn_open.config(state="disabled")
 202 |             self.btn_stop.config(state="disabled")
 203 | 
 204 |     # ── Control servidor ─────────────────────
 205 |     def _start(self):
 206 |         if not port_free(PORT):
 207 |             self._log(f"Puerto {PORT} ya en uso — conectando", "warn")
 208 |             self._set_running(True)
 209 |             self._open()
 210 |             return
 211 |         self.btn_start.config(state="disabled", text="⏳  Iniciando...", bg="#94a3b8")
 212 |         self.running = True
 213 |         threading.Thread(target=self._run_server, daemon=True).start()
 214 | 
 215 |     def _run_server(self):
 216 |         py = get_python()
 217 |         self._log(f"Python: {py}")
 218 | 
 219 |         for d in ["database", "logs", "invoices", "supplier_docs"]:
 220 |             os.makedirs(d, exist_ok=True)
 221 | 
 222 |         if Path("requirements.txt").exists():
 223 |             self._log("Verificando dependencias...")
 224 |             try:
 225 |                 subprocess.run([py, "-m", "pip", "install", "-r", "requirements.txt", "-q"],
 226 |                                capture_output=True, timeout=180)
 227 |                 self._log("Dependencias OK", "ok")
 228 |             except Exception as e:
 229 |                 self._log(f"pip: {e}", "warn")
 230 | 
 231 |         self._log(f"Iniciando servidor en :{PORT}...")
 232 |         try:
 233 |             flags = subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW if sys.platform == "win32" else 0
 234 |             self.proc = subprocess.Popen(
 235 |                 [py, "-m", "uvicorn", "app.main:app",
 236 |                  "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", str(PORT), "--log-level", "warning"],
 237 |                 stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
 238 |                 text=True, creationflags=flags)
 239 |         except Exception as e:
 240 |             self._log(f"Error al iniciar: {e}", "err")
 241 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self._set_running(False))
 242 |             return
 243 | 
 244 |         if wait_server(PORT, 30):
 245 |             self._log(f"Servidor activo — {APP_URL}", "ok")
 246 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self._set_running(True))
 247 |             self.root.after(800, self._open)
 248 |         else:
 249 |             self._log("El servidor no respondió a tiempo", "err")
 250 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self._set_running(False))
 251 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self.btn_start.config(
 252 |                 state="normal", bg=C_DARK, text="▶   Iniciar Sistema"))
 253 | 
 254 |         if self.proc:
 255 |             for line in self.proc.stdout:
 256 |                 l = line.strip()
 257 |                 if l: self._log(l)
 258 | 
 259 |     def _stop(self):
 260 |         if self.proc:
 261 |             self._log("Deteniendo servidor...")
 262 |             try:
 263 |                 self.proc.terminate()
 264 |                 self.proc.wait(timeout=5)
 265 |             except Exception:
 266 |                 try: self.proc.kill()
 267 |                 except: pass
 268 |             self.proc = None
 269 |         self.running = False
 270 |         self._set_running(False)
 271 |         self._log("Servidor detenido", "ok")
 272 | 
 273 |     def _open(self):
 274 |         if not port_free(PORT):
 275 |             webbrowser.open(APP_URL)
 276 |         else:
 277 |             self._log("El servidor no está activo aún", "warn")
 278 | 
 279 |     def _close(self):
 280 |         if self.running and self.proc:
 281 |             if messagebox.askyesno("Cerrar",
 282 |                     "El servidor está activo.\n¿Deseas detenerlo y cerrar?",
 283 |                     icon="warning"):
 284 |                 self._stop()
 285 |                 self.root.destroy()
 286 |         else:
 287 |             self.root.destroy()
 288 | 
 289 |     def run(self):
 290 |         self.root.mainloop()
 291 | 
 292 | 
 293 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 294 |     os.chdir(Path(__file__).parent.resolve())
 295 |     Launcher().run()
 296 |

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: app\config.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\config.py
================================================================================

   1 | from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings, SettingsConfigDict
   2 | from pathlib import Path
   3 | 
   4 | class Settings(BaseSettings):
   5 |     DATABASE_URL: str
   6 |     SECRET_KEY: str = "1234"  #  NUEVO
   7 |     ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"  # NUEVO
   8 |     ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30  #  NUEVO
   9 |

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: app\middleware\auth_middleware.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\middleware\auth_middleware.py
================================================================================

   1 | from fastapi import Request, HTTPException
   2 | from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials
   3 | from jose import jwt, JWTError
   4 | from starlette.middleware.base import BaseHTTPMiddleware
   5 | from starlette.responses import RedirectResponse
   6 | import re
   7 | 
   8 | from app.config import settings
   9 | 
  10 | security = HTTPBearer(auto_error=False)
  11 | 
  12 | class AuthMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
  13 |     async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next):
  14 |         # Rutas públicas (no requieren token)
  15 |         public_paths = [
  16 |             r'^/login$',
  17 |             r'^/static/.*',
  18 |             r'^/auth/token$',
  19 |             r'^/auth/login$',
  20 |             r'^/$'
  21 |         ]
  22 |         
  23 |         path = request.url.path
  24 |         
  25 |         # Verificar si es ruta pública
  26 |         for pattern in public_paths:
  27 |             if re.match(pattern, path):
  28 |                 return await call_next(request)
  29 |         
  30 |         # Verificar token
  31 |         token = request.headers.get("Authorization")
  32 |         if not token:
  33 |             # Si no hay token, redirigir al login
  34 |             return RedirectResponse(url="/login")
  35 |         
  36 |         try:
  37 |             token = token.replace("Bearer ", "")
  38 |             payload = jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
  39 |             request.state.user = payload
  40 |         except JWTError:
  41 |             return RedirectResponse(url="/login")
  42 |         
  43 |         return await call_next(request)

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: app\reports\pdf_generator.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\reports\pdf_generator.py
================================================================================

   1 | import os
   2 | from jinja2 import Environment, FileSystemLoader
   3 | 
   4 | 
   5 | def generate_invoice_pdf(data: dict, output_path: str):
   6 |     """
   7 |     Genera un PDF de factura usando Jinja2 + WeasyPrint.
   8 |     ✅ CORREGIDO: reemplaza la implementación con ReportLab que no usaba
   9 |     la plantilla HTML ni pasaba variables dinámicas correctamente.
  10 |     """
  11 | 
  12 |     # Intentar con WeasyPrint (requiere: pip install weasyprint)
  13 |     try:
  14 |         import weasyprint
  15 | 
  16 |         template_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "templates")
  17 |         template_dir = os.path.abspath(template_dir)
  18 | 
  19 |         env = Environment(loader=FileSystemLoader(template_dir))
  20 |         template = env.get_template("invoice_template.html")
  21 | 
  22 |         html_content = template.render(**data)
  23 | 
  24 |         weasyprint.HTML(string=html_content).write_pdf(output_path)
  25 | 
  26 |     except ImportError:
  27 |         # Fallback: si WeasyPrint no está instalado, genera HTML y lo guarda como .html
  28 |         # Útil para desarrollo. En producción instalar: pip install weasyprint
  29 |         template_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "templates")
  30 |         template_dir = os.path.abspath(template_dir)
  31 | 
  32 |         env = Environment(loader=FileSystemLoader(template_dir))
  33 |         template = env.get_template("invoice_template.html")
  34 |         html_content = template.render(**data)
  35 | 
  36 |         html_path = output_path.replace(".pdf", ".html")
  37 |         with open(html_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
  38 |             f.write(html_content)
  39 | 
  40 |         print(f"[AVISO] WeasyPrint no instalado. Factura guardada como HTML: {html_path}")
  41 |         print("Para generar PDFs reales ejecutar: pip install weasyprint")
  42 | 
  43 |     return output_path
  44 |

  32 | @router.get("/upcoming")

  34 |     """Próximos eventos desde hoy (para el dashboard)."""
  35 |     from datetime import date as dt
  36 |     return db.query(AgendaEvent).filter(
  37 |         AgendaEvent.event_date >= dt.today(),
  38 |         AgendaEvent.status == "PENDIENTE"

  45 |     return ev

  50 |     if not ev:
  51 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Evento no encontrado")
  52 |     for k, v in data.dict().items():

  54 |     db.commit(); db.refresh(ev)
  55 |     return ev

   1 | from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status
   2 | from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer, OAuth2PasswordRequestForm
   3 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
   4 | from datetime import timedelta
   5 | 
   6 | from app.database import get_db
   7 | from app.models.user import User
   8 | from app.services.security import verify_password
   9 | from app.services.auth_service import create_access_token, authenticate_user, get_current_user
  10 | from app.schemas.auth_schema import LoginResponse, UserResponse
  11 | from app.config import settings
  12 | 
  13 | router = APIRouter(prefix="/auth", tags=["Authentication"])
  14 | oauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="/auth/token")
  15 | 
  16 | @router.post("/token", response_model=LoginResponse)
  17 | async def login_for_access_token(
  18 |     form_data: OAuth2PasswordRequestForm = Depends(),
  19 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  20 | ):
  21 |     """
  22 |     Endpoint estándar OAuth2 para obtener token.
  23 |     Accepta form-data con username y password.
  24 |     """
  25 |     user = authenticate_user(db, form_data.username, form_data.password)
  26 |     
  27 |     if not user:
  28 |         raise HTTPException(
  29 |             status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
  30 |             detail="Usuario o contraseña incorrectos",
  31 |             headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
  32 |         )
  33 |     
  34 |     access_token_expires = timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
  35 |     access_token = create_access_token(
  36 |         data={"sub": user.username, "role": user.role},
  37 |         expires_delta=access_token_expires
  38 |     )
  39 |     
  40 |     return {
  41 |         "access_token": access_token,
  42 |         "token_type": "bearer",
  43 |         "username": user.username,
  44 |         "role": user.role
  45 |     }
  46 | 
  47 | @router.post("/login", response_model=LoginResponse)
  48 | async def login_json(
  49 |     login_data: dict,
  50 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  51 | ):
  52 |     """
  53 |     Endpoint alternativo que acepta JSON para login.
  54 |     """
  55 |     username = login_data.get("username")
  56 |     password = login_data.get("password")
  57 |     
  58 |     if not username or not password:
  59 |         raise HTTPException(
  60 |             status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
  61 |             detail="Username y password son requeridos"
  62 |         )
  63 |     
  64 |     user = authenticate_user(db, username, password)
  65 |     
  66 |     if not user:
  67 |         raise HTTPException(
  68 |             status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
  69 |             detail="Usuario o contraseña incorrectos"
  70 |         )
  71 |     
  72 |     access_token_expires = timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
  73 |     access_token = create_access_token(
  74 |         data={"sub": user.username, "role": user.role},
  75 |         expires_delta=access_token_expires
  76 |     )
  77 |     
  78 |     return {
  79 |         "access_token": access_token,
  80 |         "token_type": "bearer",
  81 |         "username": user.username,
  82 |         "role": user.role
  83 |     }
  84 | 
  85 | @router.get("/me", response_model=UserResponse)
  86 | async def read_users_me(
  87 |     token: str = Depends(oauth2_scheme),
  88 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  89 | ):
  90 |     """Obtiene información del usuario actual"""
  91 |     current_user = get_current_user(token, db)
  92 |     return current_user

  94 | # Dependencia para verificar si el usuario es admin
  95 | def get_current_admin(
  96 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)
  97 | ):
  98 |     if current_user.role != "ADMIN":
  99 |         raise HTTPException(
 100 |             status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,
 101 |             detail="Se requieren privilegios de administrador"
 102 |         )
 103 |     return current_user

 105 | from pydantic import BaseModel as _BaseModel
 106 | from typing import Optional as _Optional
 107 | 
 108 | 
 109 | class UserCreate(_BaseModel):
 110 |     username: str
 111 |     password: str
 112 |     role: str = "USER"   # ADMIN | USER
 113 | 
 114 | 
 115 | class UserPasswordChange(_BaseModel):
 116 |     new_password: str
 117 | 
 118 | 
 119 | # ── Listar todos los usuarios — solo ADMIN ────────────────
 120 | @router.get("/users")
 121 | def list_users(
 122 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 123 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 124 | ):
 125 |     users = db.query(User).order_by(User.username).all()
 126 |     return [
 127 |         {
 128 |             "id":        u.id,
 129 |             "username":  u.username,
 130 |             "role":      u.role,
 131 |             "is_active": u.is_active,
 132 |         }
 133 |         for u in users
 134 |     ]
 135 | 
 136 | 
 137 | # ── Crear usuario — solo ADMIN ────────────────────────────
 138 | @router.post("/users")
 139 | def create_user(
 140 |     data: UserCreate,
 141 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 142 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 143 | ):
 144 |     from app.services.security import hash_password
 145 | 
 146 |     if data.role not in ("ADMIN", "USER"):
 147 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Rol inválido. Usa ADMIN o USER")
 148 | 
 149 |     exists = db.query(User).filter(User.username == data.username).first()
 150 |     if exists:
 151 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El nombre de usuario ya existe")
 152 | 
 153 |     new_user = User(
 154 |         username      = data.username,
 155 |         password_hash = hash_password(data.password),
 156 |         role          = data.role,
 157 |         is_active     = True,
 158 |     )
 159 |     db.add(new_user)
 160 |     db.commit()
 161 |     db.refresh(new_user)
 162 |     return {"message": "Usuario creado", "id": new_user.id, "username": new_user.username, "role": new_user.role}
 163 | 
 164 | 
 165 | # ── Activar / Desactivar usuario — solo ADMIN ─────────────
 166 | @router.patch("/users/{user_id}/toggle")
 167 | def toggle_user(
 168 |     user_id: int,
 169 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 170 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 171 | ):
 172 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.id == user_id).first()
 173 |     if not user:
 174 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Usuario no encontrado")
 175 |     if user.username == current_user.username:
 176 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No puedes desactivarte a ti mismo")
 177 | 
 178 |     user.is_active = not user.is_active
 179 |     db.commit()
 180 |     return {"message": f"Usuario {'activado' if user.is_active else 'desactivado'}", "is_active": user.is_active}
 181 | 
 182 | 
 183 | # ── Cambiar contraseña de un usuario — solo ADMIN ─────────
 184 | @router.patch("/users/{user_id}/password")
 185 | def change_user_password(
 186 |     user_id: int,
 187 |     data: UserPasswordChange,
 188 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 189 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 190 | ):
 191 |     from app.services.security import hash_password
 192 | 
 193 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.id == user_id).first()
 194 |     if not user:
 195 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Usuario no encontrado")
 196 |     if not data.new_password or len(data.new_password) < 6:
 197 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres")
 198 | 
 199 |     user.password_hash = hash_password(data.new_password)
 200 |     db.commit()
 201 |     return {"message": "Contraseña actualizada correctamente"}
 202 | 
 203 | 
 204 | # ── Eliminar usuario — solo ADMIN ─────────────────────────
 205 | @router.delete("/users/{user_id}")
 206 | def delete_user(
 207 |     user_id: int,
 208 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 209 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 210 | ):
 211 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.id == user_id).first()
 212 |     if not user:
 213 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Usuario no encontrado")
 214 |     if user.username == current_user.username:
 215 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No puedes eliminar tu propia cuenta")
 216 | 
 217 |     db.delete(user)
 218 |     db.commit()
 219 |     return {"message": "Usuario eliminado"}

   1 | """
   2 | app/routers/charges.py  v2
   3 | Agrega:
   4 |   PUT  /charges/{charge_id}   — editar cargo (solo ADMIN)
   5 |   DELETE /charges/{charge_id} — eliminar cargo (solo ADMIN)
   6 | """
   7 | 
   8 | from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
   9 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
  10 | 
  11 | from app.models.charge import Charge
  12 | from app.models.unit import Unit
  13 | from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
  14 | from app.schemas.charge import ChargeCreate, ChargeResponse
  15 | from app.database import get_db
  16 | from app.services.auth_service import get_current_user
  17 | from app.models.user import User
  18 | 
  19 | router = APIRouter(prefix="/charges", tags=["Charges"])
  20 | 
  21 | 
  22 | def _require_admin(current_user: User):
  23 |     if current_user.role != "ADMIN":
  24 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Solo el administrador puede realizar esta acción")
  25 | 
  26 | 
  27 | @router.post("/", response_model=ChargeResponse)
  28 | def create_charge(
  29 |     charge_data: ChargeCreate,
  30 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
  31 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),
  32 | ):
  33 |     unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == charge_data.unit_id).first()
  34 |     if not unit:
  35 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Unidad no encontrada")
  36 | 
  37 |     if charge_data.amount <= 0:
  38 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto debe ser mayor a 0")
  39 | 
  40 |     if charge_data.due_date < charge_data.date_created:
  41 |         raise HTTPException(
  42 |             status_code=400,
  43 |             detail="La fecha de vencimiento no puede ser menor a la fecha de registro",
  44 |         )
  45 | 
  46 |     new_charge = Charge(
  47 |         unit_id=charge_data.unit_id,
  48 |         description=charge_data.description,
  49 |         amount=charge_data.amount,
  50 |         balance=charge_data.amount,
  51 |         status="PENDIENTE",
  52 |         date_created=charge_data.date_created,
  53 |         due_date=charge_data.due_date,
  54 |     )
  55 |     db.add(new_charge)
  56 |     db.commit()
  57 |     db.refresh(new_charge)
  58 |     return new_charge
  59 | 
  60 | 
  61 | @router.put("/{charge_id}")
  62 | def update_charge(
  63 |     charge_id: int,
  64 |     charge_data: ChargeCreate,
  65 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
  66 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),
  67 | ):
  68 |     """Editar un cargo existente — solo ADMIN."""
  69 |     _require_admin(current_user)
  70 | 
  71 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
  72 |     if not charge:
  73 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cargo no encontrado")
  74 | 
  75 |     if charge_data.amount <= 0:
  76 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto debe ser mayor a 0")
  77 | 
  78 |     if charge_data.due_date < charge_data.date_created:
  79 |         raise HTTPException(
  80 |             status_code=400,
  81 |             detail="La fecha de vencimiento no puede ser menor a la fecha de registro",
  82 |         )
  83 | 
  84 |     from decimal import Decimal
  85 |     from sqlalchemy import func
  86 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
  87 | 
  88 |     # Calcular ya aplicado
  89 |     applied = db.query(
  90 |         func.coalesce(func.sum(PaymentApplication.applied_amount), 0)
  91 |     ).filter(PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge_id).scalar()
  92 | 
  93 |     new_amount  = Decimal(str(charge_data.amount))
  94 |     new_balance = new_amount - Decimal(str(applied))
  95 | 
  96 |     charge.description  = charge_data.description
  97 |     charge.amount       = new_amount
  98 |     charge.balance      = max(new_balance, Decimal("0.00"))
  99 |     charge.date_created = charge_data.date_created
 100 |     charge.due_date     = charge_data.due_date
 101 | 
 102 |     # Recalcular estado
 103 |     if new_balance <= 0:
 104 |         charge.status = "PAGADO"
 105 |     elif applied > 0:
 106 |         charge.status = "PARCIAL"
 107 |     else:
 108 |         charge.status = "PENDIENTE"
 109 | 
 110 |     db.commit()
 111 |     db.refresh(charge)
 112 |     return charge
 113 | 
 114 | 
 115 | @router.delete("/{charge_id}")
 116 | def delete_charge(
 117 |     charge_id: int,
 118 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 119 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),
 120 | ):
 121 |     """Eliminar un cargo y sus aplicaciones de pago — solo ADMIN."""
 122 |     _require_admin(current_user)
 123 | 
 124 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
 125 |     if not charge:
 126 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cargo no encontrado")
 127 | 
 128 |     # Eliminar aplicaciones asociadas primero
 129 |     db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 130 |         PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge_id
 131 |     ).delete()
 132 |     db.delete(charge)
 133 |     db.commit()
 134 |     return {"message": "Cargo eliminado correctamente"}
 135 |

 168 | @router.get("/invoices/{invoice_id}/download")
 169 | def download_invoice(invoice_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 170 |     """Descargar PDF de factura"""
 171 |     invoice = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.id == invoice_id).first()
 172 |     if not invoice or not invoice.pdf_path:
 173 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Factura no encontrada")

 176 |     import os

 179 |         return FileResponse(
 180 |             invoice.pdf_path,
 181 |             media_type="application/pdf",
 182 |             filename=f"factura_{invoice.invoice_number}.pdf",
 183 |         )
 184 |     raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Archivo PDF no encontrado")

 186 | @router.get("/payments-history")
 187 | def payments_history(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 188 |     """
 189 |     Devuelve todos los pagos del sistema con detalle completo.
 190 |     Separa concepto de observación interna.
 191 |     """
 192 |     from app.models.payment import Payment
 193 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 194 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 195 |     from app.models.unit import Unit
 196 |     from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
 197 |     from app.models.owner import Owner
 198 | 
 199 |     payments = db.query(Payment).order_by(Payment.payment_date.desc()).all()
 200 |     result   = []
 201 | 
 202 |     for p in payments:
 203 |         owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == p.owner_id).first() if p.owner_id else None
 204 | 
 205 |         # Unidad activa del propietario
 206 |         unit_number = None
 207 |         if p.owner_id:
 208 |             uo = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 209 |                 UnitOwner.owner_id == p.owner_id,
 210 |                 UnitOwner.is_active == True
 211 |             ).first()
 212 |             if uo:
 213 |                 u = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == uo.unit_id).first()
 214 |                 if u:
 215 |                     unit_number = u.unit_number
 216 | 
 217 |         # Aplicaciones (cargos vinculados)
 218 |         apps = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 219 |             PaymentApplication.payment_id == p.id
 220 |         ).all()
 221 | 
 222 |         # Concepto: si tiene cargos vinculados usa la descripción del cargo
 223 |         # Si no, usa la primera parte del campo reference (antes del " — ")
 224 |         concepto    = None
 225 |         observacion = None
 226 | 
 227 |         if apps:
 228 |             descs = []
 229 |             for app in apps:
 230 |                 c = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 231 |                 if c:
 232 |                     descs.append(c.description)
 233 |             if descs:
 234 |                 concepto = " / ".join(set(descs))
 235 | 
 236 |         if not concepto:
 237 |             ref = p.reference or ""
 238 |             if " — " in ref:
 239 |                 partes      = ref.split(" — ", 1)
 240 |                 concepto    = partes[0].strip()
 241 |                 observacion = partes[1].strip()
 242 |             else:
 243 |                 concepto    = ref.strip() or "—"
 244 |                 observacion = None
 245 | 
 246 |         result.append({
 247 |             "payment_id":    p.id,
 248 |             "factura":       p.invoice_number,
 249 |             "fecha":         str(p.payment_date) if p.payment_date else None,
 250 |             "owner_id":      p.owner_id,
 251 |             "owner_name":    owner.full_name if owner else "—",
 252 |             "unit_number":   unit_number or "—",
 253 |             "concepto":      concepto or "—",
 254 |             "observacion":   observacion,   # solo uso interno, no aparece en reportes
 255 |             "monto":         float(p.amount) if p.amount else 0,
 256 |             "referencia":    p.reference,
 257 |             "tiene_cargos":  len(apps) > 0,
 258 |         })
 259 | 
 260 |     return result
 261 | 
 262 | # ── Parche ───────────────
 263 | # ── Schemas adicionales ──────────────────────────────────────
 264 | 
 265 | class PaymentUpdate(BaseModel):
 266 |     payment_date:   date
 267 |     amount:         float
 268 |     invoice_number: Optional[str] = None
 269 |     reference:      Optional[str] = None

 272 | # ── Dependencia admin (ya existe en auth.py, aquí la redefinimos localmente) ──
 273 | def _admin_only(
 274 |     current_user = Depends(get_current_user_dep),
 275 | ):
 276 |     if current_user.role != "ADMIN":
 277 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Solo el administrador puede realizar esta acción")
 278 |     return current_user
 279 | 
 280 | 
 281 | # ── Editar pago — solo ADMIN ─────────────────────────────────
 282 | @router.put("/payment/{payment_id}")
 283 | def update_payment(
 284 |     payment_id: int,
 285 |     data: PaymentUpdate,
 286 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 287 |     current_user = Depends(_admin_only),
 288 | ):
 289 |     """Editar fecha, monto, factura y referencia de un pago. Solo ADMIN."""
 290 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 291 |     if not payment:
 292 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 293 | 
 294 |     from decimal import Decimal
 295 |     payment.payment_date   = data.payment_date
 296 |     payment.amount         = Decimal(str(data.amount))
 297 |     payment.invoice_number = data.invoice_number
 298 |     payment.reference      = data.reference
 299 |     db.commit()
 300 |     db.refresh(payment)
 301 |     return {"message": "Pago actualizado", "payment_id": payment.id}
 302 | 
 303 | 
 304 | # ── Eliminar pago — solo ADMIN ───────────────────────────────
 305 | @router.delete("/payment/{payment_id}")
 306 | def delete_payment(
 307 |     payment_id: int,
 308 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 309 |     current_user = Depends(_admin_only),
 310 | ):
 311 |     """
 312 |     Elimina un pago y revierte los saldos de los cargos afectados.
 313 |     Solo ADMIN.
 314 |     """
 315 |     from decimal import Decimal
 316 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 317 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 318 | 
 319 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 320 |     if not payment:
 321 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 322 | 
 323 |     # Revertir saldos de los cargos afectados
 324 |     apps = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 325 |         PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment_id
 326 |     ).all()
 327 | 
 328 |     for app in apps:
 329 |         charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 330 |         if charge:
 331 |             charge.balance = Decimal(str(charge.balance)) + Decimal(str(app.applied_amount))
 332 |             # Recalcular estado
 333 |             if charge.balance >= Decimal(str(charge.amount)):
 334 |                 charge.status = "PENDIENTE"
 335 |             else:
 336 |                 charge.status = "PARCIAL"
 337 |         db.delete(app)
 338 | 
 339 |     db.delete(payment)
 340 |     db.commit()
 341 |     return {"message": "Pago eliminado y saldos revertidos correctamente"}
 342 | 
 343 | 
 344 | # ── Endpoint para que admin vea todos los pagos ───────────────
 345 | @router.get("/all-payments")
 346 | def get_all_payments(
 347 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 348 |     current_user = Depends(_admin_only),
 349 | ):
 350 |     """Lista todos los pagos con detalle — solo ADMIN."""
 351 |     from app.models.owner import Owner
 352 |     from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
 353 |     from app.models.unit import Unit
 354 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 355 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 356 | 
 357 |     payments = db.query(Payment).order_by(Payment.payment_date.desc()).all()
 358 |     result   = []
 359 | 
 360 |     for p in payments:
 361 |         owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == p.owner_id).first()
 362 |         uo    = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 363 |             UnitOwner.owner_id == p.owner_id, UnitOwner.is_active == True
 364 |         ).first()
 365 |         unit  = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == uo.unit_id).first() if uo else None
 366 | 
 367 |         apps  = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 368 |             PaymentApplication.payment_id == p.id
 369 |         ).all()
 370 |         cargos = []
 371 |         for a in apps:
 372 |             c = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == a.charge_id).first()
 373 |             if c:
 374 |                 cargos.append({"description": c.description, "applied": float(a.applied_amount)})
 375 | 
 376 |         result.append({
 377 |             "payment_id":    p.id,
 378 |             "fecha":         str(p.payment_date),
 379 |             "owner_name":    owner.full_name if owner else "—",
 380 |             "unit_number":   unit.unit_number if unit else "—",
 381 |             "amount":        float(p.amount),
 382 |             "invoice_number":p.invoice_number,
 383 |             "reference":     p.reference,
 384 |             "cargos":        cargos,
 385 |         })
 386 | 
 387 |     return result

  94 | # Registrar ocupante en unidad de propiedad
  95 | @router.post("/{property_id}/register-occupant")
  96 | def register_occupant(
  97 |     property_id: int,
  98 |     data: RegisterOccupant,
  99 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
 100 | ):
 101 |     try:
 102 |         property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
 103 |         if not property_obj:
 104 |             raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
 105 | 
 106 |         # Buscar o crear unidad
 107 |         unit = db.query(Unit).filter(
 108 |             Unit.property_id == property_id,
 109 |             Unit.unit_number == data.unit_number
 110 |         ).first()
 111 | 
 112 |         if not unit:
 113 |             unit = Unit(
 114 |                 property_id=property_id,
 115 |                 unit_number=data.unit_number,
 116 |                 floor=data.floor
 117 |             )
 118 |             db.add(unit)
 119 |             db.flush()
 120 | 
 121 |         # Verificar ocupación activa
 122 |         active = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 123 |             UnitOwner.unit_id == unit.id,
 124 |             UnitOwner.is_active == True
 125 |         ).first()
 126 | 
 127 |         if active:
 128 |             raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="La unidad ya está ocupada")
 129 | 
 130 |         # Crear propietario
 131 |         owner = Owner(
 132 |             full_name=data.full_name,
 133 |             identification=data.identification,
 134 |             email=data.email,
 135 |             phone=data.phone
 136 |         )
 137 |         db.add(owner)
 138 |         db.flush()
 139 | 
 140 |         # Crear relación
 141 |         occupancy = UnitOwner(
 142 |             unit_id=unit.id,
 143 |             owner_id=owner.id,
 144 |             start_date=data.start_date,
 145 |             is_active=True
 146 |         )
 147 |         db.add(occupancy)
 148 | 
 149 |         db.commit()
 150 | 
 151 |         return {"message": "Ocupante registrado correctamente"}
 152 | 
 153 |     except SQLAlchemyError:
 154 |         db.rollback()
 155 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Error interno")
 156 |

  62 |     result = []

  66 |         ).scalar() or 0

  69 |         ).scalar() or 0

  94 |     for k, v in data.dict().items(): setattr(s, k, v)
  95 |     db.commit(); db.refresh(s); return s

 104 | # ── Detalle completo de un proveedor ─────────
 105 | @router.get("/{supplier_id}/detail")
 106 | def supplier_detail(supplier_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 107 |     s = db.query(Supplier).filter(Supplier.id == supplier_id, Supplier.is_active == True).first()
 108 |     if not s: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Proveedor no encontrado")
 109 | 
 110 |     payments = db.query(SupplierPayment).filter(
 111 |         SupplierPayment.supplier_id == supplier_id
 112 |     ).order_by(SupplierPayment.payment_date.desc()).all()
 113 | 
 114 |     quotes = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(
 115 |         SupplierQuote.supplier_id == supplier_id
 116 |     ).order_by(SupplierQuote.quote_date.desc()).all()
 117 | 
 118 |     total_paid    = sum(float(p.amount) for p in payments if p.status == "PAGADO")
 119 |     total_pending = sum(float(p.amount) for p in payments if p.status == "PENDIENTE")
 120 | 
 121 |     return {
 122 |         "id": s.id, "name": s.name, "category": s.category,
 123 |         "ruc": s.ruc, "contact_name": s.contact_name,
 124 |         "phone": s.phone, "email": s.email,
 125 |         "address": s.address, "notes": s.notes,
 126 |         "total_paid": total_paid, "total_pending": total_pending,
 127 |         "payments": [{
 128 |             "id": p.id, "description": p.description,
 129 |             "amount": float(p.amount), "payment_date": str(p.payment_date),
 130 |             "status": p.status, "reference": p.reference,
 131 |         } for p in payments],
 132 |         "quotes": [{
 133 |             "id": q.id, "description": q.description,
 134 |             "amount": float(q.amount), "quote_date": str(q.quote_date),
 135 |             "valid_until": str(q.valid_until) if q.valid_until else None,
 136 |             "status": q.status, "notes": q.notes,
 137 |             "pdf_path": q.pdf_path if hasattr(q, 'pdf_path') else None,

 201 | def delete_quote(quote_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 202 |     q = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(SupplierQuote.id == quote_id).first()
 203 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 204 |     # Eliminar PDF si existe
 205 |     if getattr(q, 'pdf_path', None) and os.path.exists(q.pdf_path):
 206 |         os.remove(q.pdf_path)

 210 | # ── Upload PDF de cotización ──────────────────
 211 | @router.post("/quotes/{quote_id}/upload-pdf")
 212 | async def upload_quote_pdf(
 213 |     quote_id: int,
 214 |     file: UploadFile = File(...),
 215 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
 216 | ):
 217 |     q = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(SupplierQuote.id == quote_id).first()
 218 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 219 | 
 220 |     # Validar que sea PDF
 221 |     if not file.content_type == "application/pdf" and not file.filename.lower().endswith(".pdf"):
 222 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Solo se aceptan archivos PDF")
 223 | 
 224 |     # Eliminar PDF anterior si existe
 225 |     if getattr(q, 'pdf_path', None) and os.path.exists(q.pdf_path):
 226 |         os.remove(q.pdf_path)
 227 | 
 228 |     # Guardar nuevo PDF
 229 |     filename    = f"quote_{quote_id}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}.pdf"
 230 |     file_path   = os.path.join(PDF_DIR, filename)
 231 | 
 232 |     with open(file_path, "wb") as f:
 233 |         shutil.copyfileobj(file.file, f)
 234 | 
 235 |     q.pdf_path = file_path
 236 |     db.commit()
 237 | 
 238 |     return {"message": "PDF subido correctamente", "pdf_path": file_path}
 239 | 
 240 | # ── Descargar PDF de cotización ───────────────
 241 | @router.get("/quotes/{quote_id}/pdf")
 242 | def download_quote_pdf(quote_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 243 |     q = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(SupplierQuote.id == quote_id).first()
 244 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 245 | 
 246 |     pdf_path = getattr(q, 'pdf_path', None)
 247 |     if not pdf_path or not os.path.exists(pdf_path):
 248 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="PDF no encontrado")
 249 | 
 250 |     return FileResponse(
 251 |         pdf_path,
 252 |         media_type="application/pdf",
 253 |         filename=f"cotizacion_{quote_id}.pdf"

  20 | @router.post("/")

  22 |     data: UnitOwnerCreate,
  23 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  24 | ):
  25 |     unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == data.unit_id).first()
  26 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == data.owner_id).first()
  27 | 
  28 |     if not unit:
  29 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Unidad no encontrada")
  30 | 
  31 |     if not owner:
  32 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propietario no encontrado")
  33 |

  35 |     active_ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
  36 |         UnitOwner.unit_id == data.unit_id,

  38 |     ).first()

  49 |     )

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: app\services\auth_service.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\services\auth_service.py
================================================================================

   1 | """
   2 | app/services/auth_service.py
   3 | JWT + creación de usuario admin por defecto al arrancar.
   4 | """
   5 | 
   6 | from datetime import datetime, timedelta
   7 | from typing import Optional
   8 | 
   9 | from fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status
  10 | from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer
  11 | from jose import JWTError, jwt
  12 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
  13 | 
  14 | from app.config import settings
  15 | from app.database import get_db
  16 | from app.models.user import User
  17 | from app.services.security import verify_password, hash_password
  18 | 
  19 | oauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="/api/auth/token")
  20 | 
  21 | 
  22 | # ── JWT ──────────────────────────────────────
  23 | def create_access_token(data: dict, expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:
  24 |     payload = data.copy()
  25 |     payload["exp"] = datetime.utcnow() + (expires_delta or timedelta(minutes=60))
  26 |     return jwt.encode(payload, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)
  27 | 
  28 | 
  29 | def decode_token(token: str) -> Optional[dict]:
  30 |     try:
  31 |         return jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
  32 |     except JWTError:
  33 |         return None
  34 | 
  35 | 
  36 | # ── Autenticar ───────────────────────────────
  37 | def authenticate_user(db: Session, username: str, password: str) -> Optional[User]:
  38 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()
  39 |     if not user or not user.is_active:
  40 |         return None
  41 |     if not verify_password(password, user.password_hash):
  42 |         return None
  43 |     return user
  44 | 
  45 | 
  46 | # ── get_current_user (dependencia FastAPI) ────
  47 | def get_current_user(
  48 |     token: str = Depends(oauth2_scheme),
  49 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
  50 | ) -> User:
  51 |     exc = HTTPException(
  52 |         status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
  53 |         detail="Sesión inválida o expirada",
  54 |         headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
  55 |     )
  56 |     payload = decode_token(token)
  57 |     if not payload:
  58 |         raise exc
  59 |     username = payload.get("sub")
  60 |     if not username:
  61 |         raise exc
  62 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()
  63 |     if not user or not user.is_active:
  64 |         raise exc
  65 |     return user
  66 | 
  67 | 
  68 | # ── Crear admin por defecto al arrancar ───────
  69 | def create_default_admin(db: Session):
  70 |     """
  71 |     Se llama desde app/main.py al iniciar.
  72 |     Crea el usuario admin si no existe usando las variables del .env:
  73 |       DEFAULT_ADMIN_USER / DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASS
  74 |     """
  75 |     import os
  76 |     username = getattr(settings, "DEFAULT_ADMIN_USER", "admin")
  77 |     password = getattr(settings, "DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASS", "Admin123")
  78 | 
  79 |     if not db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first():
  80 |         db.add(User(
  81 |             username=username,
  82 |             password_hash=hash_password(password),
  83 |             role="ADMIN",
  84 |             is_active=True,
  85 |         ))
  86 |         db.commit()
  87 |         print(f"[AUTH] Usuario admin creado: {username}")
  88 |

ARCHIVO: app\services\finance_service.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\services\finance_service.py
================================================================================

   1 | from datetime import date
   2 | from decimal import Decimal, ROUND_HALF_UP
   3 | import os
   4 | 
   5 | from fastapi import HTTPException
   6 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
   7 | from sqlalchemy import func
   8 | 
   9 | from app.models.charge import Charge
  10 | from app.models.payment import Payment
  11 | from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
  12 | from app.models.owner import Owner
  13 | from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
  14 | from app.models.unit import Unit
  15 | from app.models.property import Property
  16 | from app.models.invoice import Invoice
  17 | 
  18 | 
  19 | def _to_dec(val) -> Decimal:
  20 |     """Convierte cualquier valor numérico a Decimal de forma segura."""
  21 |     return Decimal(str(val)).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
  22 | 
  23 | 
  24 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  25 | # Función 1 — Balance de un cargo específico
  26 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  27 | def get_charge_balance(db: Session, charge_id: int):
  28 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
  29 | 
  30 |     if not charge:
  31 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cargo no encontrado")
  32 | 
  33 |     total_applied_raw = (
  34 |         db.query(func.coalesce(func.sum(PaymentApplication.applied_amount), 0))
  35 |         .filter(PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge_id)
  36 |         .scalar()
  37 |     )
  38 | 
  39 |     # ✅ Todo en Decimal para evitar errores float vs Decimal (SQLite y PostgreSQL)
  40 |     amount       = _to_dec(charge.amount)
  41 |     total_applied = _to_dec(total_applied_raw)
  42 |     balance      = amount - total_applied
  43 | 
  44 |     return {
  45 |         "charge_id":      charge.id,
  46 |         "total_amount":   amount,
  47 |         "applied_amount": total_applied,
  48 |         "balance":        balance,
  49 |     }
  50 | 
  51 | 
  52 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  53 | # Función 2 — Estado textual de un cargo
  54 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  55 | def get_charge_status(db: Session, charge_id: int) -> str:
  56 |     bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge_id)
  57 | 
  58 |     if bd["applied_amount"] == Decimal("0.00"):
  59 |         return "PENDIENTE"
  60 |     elif bd["balance"] > Decimal("0.00"):
  61 |         return "PARCIAL"
  62 |     else:
  63 |         return "PAGADO"
  64 | 
  65 | 
  66 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  67 | # Función 3 — Aplicar pago a un cargo individual
  68 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  69 | def apply_payment_to_charge(db: Session, payment_id: int, charge_id: int, amount: float):
  70 |     amount_dec = _to_dec(amount)
  71 | 
  72 |     if amount_dec <= Decimal("0.00"):
  73 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto debe ser mayor a 0")
  74 | 
  75 |     charge_balance   = get_charge_balance(db, charge_id)
  76 |     payment_balance  = _to_dec(get_payment_balance(db, payment_id))
  77 | 
  78 |     if amount_dec > charge_balance["balance"]:
  79 |         raise HTTPException(
  80 |             status_code=400,
  81 |             detail=f"Monto ${float(amount_dec):.2f} supera el saldo del cargo (${float(charge_balance['balance']):.2f})"
  82 |         )
  83 | 
  84 |     if amount_dec > payment_balance:
  85 |         raise HTTPException(
  86 |             status_code=400,
  87 |             detail=f"Saldo del pago insuficiente (disponible: ${float(payment_balance):.2f})"
  88 |         )
  89 | 
  90 |     application = PaymentApplication(
  91 |         payment_id=payment_id,
  92 |         charge_id=charge_id,
  93 |         applied_amount=amount_dec,
  94 |     )
  95 |     db.add(application)
  96 | 
  97 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
  98 |     new_balance = _to_dec(charge.balance) - amount_dec
  99 | 
 100 |     if new_balance <= Decimal("0.00"):
 101 |         charge.balance = Decimal("0.00")
 102 |         charge.status  = "PAGADO"
 103 |     else:
 104 |         charge.balance = new_balance
 105 |         charge.status  = "PARCIAL"
 106 | 
 107 |     db.commit()
 108 |     db.refresh(application)
 109 |     return application
 110 |

 112 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 113 | # Función 4 CORREGIDA — Estado de cuenta por propietario
 114 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 115 | # BUG original: el JOIN con UnitOwner sin filtro is_active=True
 116 | # devolvía duplicados o cargos de periodos anteriores.
 117 | # CORRECCIÓN: filtrar UnitOwner activos y retornar TODOS los cargos
 118 | # con sus balances reales (el frontend filtra los pendientes).
 119 | 
 120 | def get_owner_account_statement(db, owner_id: int):
 121 |     from fastapi import HTTPException
 122 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 123 |     from app.models.unit import Unit
 124 |     from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
 125 |     from app.models.owner import Owner
 126 | 
 127 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == owner_id).first()
 128 |     if not owner:
 129 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propietario no encontrado")
 130 | 
 131 |     # Obtener TODAS las unidades que alguna vez tuvo este propietario
 132 |     ownerships = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 133 |         UnitOwner.owner_id == owner_id
 134 |     ).all()
 135 | 
 136 |     unit_ids = list({o.unit_id for o in ownerships})
 137 |     if not unit_ids:
 138 |         return []
 139 | 
 140 |     charges = db.query(Charge).filter(
 141 |         Charge.unit_id.in_(unit_ids)
 142 |     ).order_by(Charge.due_date).all()
 143 | 
 144 |     result = []

 153 |             "total":       float(bd["total_amount"]),
 154 |             "paid":        float(bd["applied_amount"]),
 155 |             "balance":     float(bd["balance"]),
 156 |             "status":      get_charge_status(db, charge.id),
 157 |         })

 208 | # Función 5 — Cargo general para toda una propiedad
 209 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 210 | def create_general_charge_for_property(
 211 |     db: Session, property_id: int, description: str, amount: float, due_date: date
 212 | ):
 213 |     property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
 214 |     if not property_obj:
 215 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
 216 | 
 217 |     units = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.property_id == property_id).all()
 218 |     if not units:
 219 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="La propiedad no tiene unidades")
 220 | 
 221 |     amount_dec = _to_dec(amount)
 222 |     today      = date.today()
 223 |     created    = []
 224 | 
 225 |     for unit in units:
 226 |         charge = Charge(
 227 |             unit_id=unit.id, description=description,
 228 |             amount=amount_dec, balance=amount_dec,
 229 |             status="PENDIENTE", date_created=today, due_date=due_date,
 230 |         )
 231 |         db.add(charge)
 232 |         created.append(charge)
 233 | 
 234 |     db.commit()
 235 |     return created

 238 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 239 | # Función 6 — Resumen financiero de una propiedad
 240 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 241 | def get_property_financial_summary(db: Session, property_id: int):
 242 |     property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
 243 |     if not property_obj:
 244 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
 245 | 
 246 |     charges = (
 247 |         db.query(Charge)
 248 |         .join(Unit, Charge.unit_id == Unit.id)
 249 |         .filter(Unit.property_id == property_id)
 250 |         .all()
 251 |     )
 252 | 
 253 |     total_charged = Decimal("0.00")
 254 |     total_paid    = Decimal("0.00")
 255 | 
 256 |     for charge in charges:
 257 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 258 |         total_charged += bd["total_amount"]
 259 |         total_paid    += bd["applied_amount"]
 260 | 
 261 |     return {
 262 |         "property":      property_obj.name,
 263 |         "total_charged": float(total_charged),
 264 |         "total_paid":    float(total_paid),
 265 |         "total_pending": float(total_charged - total_paid),
 266 |     }
 267 | 
 268 | 
 269 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 270 | # Función 7 — Balance disponible de un pago
 271 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 272 | def get_payment_balance(db: Session, payment_id: int) -> float:
 273 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 274 |     if not payment:
 275 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 276 | 
 277 |     total_applied_raw = (
 278 |         db.query(func.coalesce(func.sum(PaymentApplication.applied_amount), 0))
 279 |         .filter(PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment_id)
 280 |         .scalar()
 281 |     )
 282 | 
 283 |     return float(_to_dec(payment.amount) - _to_dec(total_applied_raw))
 284 | 
 285 | 
 286 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 287 | # Función 8 — Crear pago + aplicar cargos (atómico)
 288 | # ✅ CORREGIDO: flush() en lugar de commit() parcial
 289 | # ✅ CORREGIDO: un solo commit al final — todo o nada
 290 | # ✅ CORREGIDO: Decimal en todas las comparaciones
 291 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 292 | def create_payment_with_applications(db: Session, payment_data):
 293 |     total_to_apply = _to_dec(sum(app.amount for app in payment_data.applications))
 294 |     payment_amount = _to_dec(payment_data.amount)
 295 | 
 296 |     if total_to_apply > payment_amount:
 297 |         raise HTTPException(
 298 |             status_code=400,
 299 |             detail=f"Las aplicaciones (${float(total_to_apply):.2f}) superan el monto del pago (${float(payment_amount):.2f})"
 300 |         )
 301 | 
 302 |     payment = Payment(
 303 |         owner_id=payment_data.owner_id,
 304 |         payment_date=payment_data.payment_date,
 305 |         amount=payment_amount,
 306 |         invoice_number=getattr(payment_data, "invoice_number", None),
 307 |         reference=getattr(payment_data, "reference", None),
 308 |     )
 309 | 
 310 |     try:
 311 |         db.add(payment)
 312 |         db.flush()  # ← obtiene payment.id sin cerrar la transacción
 313 | 
 314 |         for app in payment_data.applications:
 315 |             app_amount = _to_dec(app.amount)
 316 | 
 317 |             charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 318 |             if not charge:
 319 |                 raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Cargo {app.charge_id} no encontrado")
 320 | 
 321 |             charge_balance = _to_dec(charge.balance)
 322 | 
 323 |             if app_amount <= Decimal("0.00"):
 324 |                 raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto de cada aplicación debe ser mayor a 0")
 325 | 
 326 |             if app_amount > charge_balance:
 327 |                 raise HTTPException(
 328 |                     status_code=400,
 329 |                     detail=f"El monto ${float(app_amount):.2f} supera el saldo de '{charge.description}' (${float(charge_balance):.2f})"
 330 |                 )
 331 | 
 332 |             db.add(PaymentApplication(
 333 |                 payment_id=payment.id,
 334 |                 charge_id=app.charge_id,
 335 |                 applied_amount=app_amount,
 336 |             ))
 337 | 
 338 |             new_balance = charge_balance - app_amount
 339 |             if new_balance <= Decimal("0.00"):
 340 |                 charge.balance = Decimal("0.00")
 341 |                 charge.status  = "PAGADO"
 342 |             else:
 343 |                 charge.balance = new_balance
 344 |                 charge.status  = "PARCIAL"
 345 | 
 346 |         db.commit()          # ← único commit: todo o nada
 347 |         db.refresh(payment)
 348 | 
 349 |     except HTTPException:
 350 |         db.rollback()
 351 |         raise
 352 |     except Exception as e:
 353 |         db.rollback()
 354 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Error al registrar pago: {str(e)}")
 355 | 
 356 |     return payment
 357 |

 395 |             "status":      status,
 396 |             "due_date":    str(charge.due_date),
 397 |             "date_created": str(charge.date_created),

 426 | def get_payment_detail_full(db: Session, payment_id: int):
 427 |     """Obtiene detalle completo de un pago para factura"""
 428 |     from app.models import Payment, Owner, UnitOwner, Unit, Property, Invoice, PaymentApplication, Charge
 429 |     
 430 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 431 |     if not payment:
 432 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 433 |     
 434 |     # Propietario
 435 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == payment.owner_id).first()
 436 |     
 437 |     # Unidad activa del propietario
 438 |     ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 439 |         UnitOwner.owner_id == payment.owner_id,
 440 |         UnitOwner.is_active == True
 441 |     ).first()
 442 |     unit = ownership.unit if ownership else None
 443 |     property_obj = unit.property if unit else None
 444 |     
 445 |     # Factura
 446 |     invoice = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == payment_id).first()
 447 |     
 448 |     # Aplicaciones
 449 |     applications = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 450 |         PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment_id
 451 |     ).all()
 452 |     
 453 |     apps_detail = []
 454 |     for app in applications:
 455 |         charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 456 |         apps_detail.append({
 457 |             "charge_id": app.charge_id,
 458 |             "description": charge.description if charge else f"Cargo #{app.charge_id}",
 459 |             "applied_amount": float(app.applied_amount),
 460 |         })
 461 |     
 462 |     return {
 463 |         "payment_id": payment.id,
 464 |         "payment_date": str(payment.payment_date),
 465 |         "amount": float(payment.amount),
 466 |         "reference": payment.reference,
 467 |         "invoice_number": invoice.invoice_number if invoice else None,
 468 |         "fiscal_invoice_number": invoice.fiscal_invoice_number if invoice else None,
 469 |         "owner_name": owner.full_name if owner else None,
 470 |         "unit_number": unit.unit_number if unit else None,
 471 |         "property_name": property_obj.name if property_obj else None,
 472 |         "applications": apps_detail,
 473 |     }

 475 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 476 | # Función 11 — Número de factura secuencial
 477 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 478 | def generate_invoice_number(db: Session) -> str:
 479 |     last = db.query(Invoice).order_by(Invoice.id.desc()).first()
 480 |     if not last:
 481 |         return "INV-000001"
 482 |     try:
 483 |         n = int(last.invoice_number.split("-")[1])
 484 |     except (IndexError, ValueError):
 485 |         n = 0
 486 |     return f"INV-{str(n + 1).zfill(6)}"
 487 |

 489 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 490 | # Función 12 — Generar factura PDF
 491 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 492 | def create_invoice_for_payment(db: Session, payment_id: int, fiscal_number: str | None = None):
 493 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 494 |     if not payment:
 495 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 496 | 
 497 |     if db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == payment_id).first():
 498 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Este pago ya tiene factura")
 499 | 
 500 |     invoice_number = generate_invoice_number(db)
 501 |     owner          = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == payment.owner_id).first()
 502 | 
 503 |     applications = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 504 |         PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment.id
 505 |     ).all()
 506 |     if not applications:
 507 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El pago no tiene cargos aplicados")
 508 | 
 509 |     first_charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == applications[0].charge_id).first()
 510 |     unit         = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == first_charge.unit_id).first() if first_charge else None
 511 |     property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == unit.property_id).first() if unit else None
 512 | 
 513 |     charges_detail = []
 514 |     for app in applications:
 515 |         c = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 516 |         if c:
 517 |             charges_detail.append({"description": c.description, "amount": float(app.applied_amount)})
 518 | 
 519 |     data = {
 520 |         "invoice_number":       invoice_number,
 521 |         "fiscal_invoice_number": fiscal_number or "",
 522 |         "issue_date":           date.today().strftime("%d de %B, %Y"),
 523 |         "owner_name":           owner.full_name if owner else "Desconocido",
 524 |         "unit_number":          unit.unit_number if unit else "N/A",
 525 |         "building_name":        property_obj.name if property_obj else "N/A",
 526 |         "property_address":     property_obj.address if property_obj else "N/A",
 527 |         "charges":              charges_detail,
 528 |         "total_amount":         float(payment.amount),
 529 |     }
 530 | 
 531 |     os.makedirs("invoices", exist_ok=True)
 532 |     pdf_path = f"invoices/{invoice_number}.pdf"
 533 | 
 534 |     from app.reports.pdf_generator import generate_invoice_pdf
 535 |     generate_invoice_pdf(data, pdf_path)
 536 | 
 537 |     invoice = Invoice(
 538 |         invoice_number=invoice_number,
 539 |         fiscal_invoice_number=fiscal_number,
 540 |         payment_id=payment.id,
 541 |         pdf_path=pdf_path,
 542 |     )
 543 |     db.add(invoice)
 544 |     db.commit()
 545 |     db.refresh(invoice)
 546 |     return invoice

 549 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 550 | # Función 13 — Estado de cuenta detallado de un propietario
 551 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 552 | def generate_owner_statement(db: Session, owner_id: int):
 553 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == owner_id).first()
 554 |     if not owner:
 555 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propietario no encontrado")
 556 | 
 557 |     ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 558 |         UnitOwner.owner_id == owner_id,
 559 |         UnitOwner.is_active == True,
 560 |     ).first()
 561 |     if not ownership:
 562 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="No tiene unidad activa")
 563 | 
 564 |     unit         = ownership.unit
 565 |     property_obj = unit.property
 566 | 
 567 |     statement_data = []
 568 |     for charge in db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.unit_id == unit.id).all():
 569 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 570 | 
 571 |         payments_info = []
 572 |         for app in db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge.id).all():
 573 |             inv = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == app.payment_id).first()
 574 |             pmt = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == app.payment_id).first()
 575 |             payments_info.append({
 576 |                 "payment_date":          str(pmt.payment_date) if pmt else None,
 577 |                 "applied_amount":        float(app.applied_amount),
 578 |                 "fiscal_invoice_number": inv.fiscal_invoice_number if inv else None,
 579 |             })
 580 | 
 581 |         statement_data.append({
 582 |             "description": charge.description,
 583 |             "due_date":    str(charge.due_date),
 584 |             "amount":      float(bd["total_amount"]),
 585 |             "paid":        float(bd["applied_amount"]),
 586 |             "balance":     float(bd["balance"]),
 587 |             "status":      get_charge_status(db, charge.id),
 588 |             "payments":    payments_info,
 589 |         })
 590 | 
 591 |     return {
 592 |         "property_name":    property_obj.name,
 593 |         "property_address": property_obj.address,
 594 |         "owner_name":       owner.full_name,
 595 |         "unit_number":      unit.unit_number,
 596 |         "statement":        statement_data,
 597 |     }

 600 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 601 | # Función 14 — Total pendiente por propiedad
 602 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 603 | def property_accounts_receivable(db: Session, property_id: int):
 604 |     charges = (
 605 |         db.query(Charge)
 606 |         .join(Unit, Charge.unit_id == Unit.id)
 607 |         .filter(Unit.property_id == property_id)
 608 |         .all()
 609 |     )
 610 |     total = Decimal("0.00")
 611 |     for charge in charges:
 612 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 613 |         total += bd["balance"]
 614 |     return {"property_id": property_id, "total_pending": float(total)}
