 351 | <div id="notification"></div>
 352 | <script src="js/main.js"></script>
 353 | <script>
 354 | renderSidebar('admin');
 355 | 
 356 | // Verificar que sea admin
 357 | if (!Auth.isAdmin()) {
 358 |   document.getElementById('access-denied').style.display = 'block';
 359 | } else {
 360 |   document.getElementById('admin-content').style.display = 'block';
 361 |   init();
 362 | }
 363 | 
 364 | let allUsers    = [];
 365 | let allPayments = [];
 366 | let allCharges  = [];
 367 | let pwdTargetId = null;
 368 | 
 369 | // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
 370 | async function init() {
 371 |   await Promise.all([loadUsers(), loadPayments(), loadCharges()]);
 372 | }
 373 | 
 374 | // ── Tabs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
 375 | function switchTab(tab) {
 376 |   document.querySelectorAll('.adm-tab').forEach((b, i) => {
 377 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['usuarios','pagos','cargos'][i] === tab);
 378 |   });
 379 |   document.querySelectorAll('.adm-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 380 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 381 | }
 382 | 
 383 | // ════════════ USUARIOS ════════════════════════════════════
 384 | 
 385 | async function loadUsers() {
 386 |   allUsers = await apiRequest('/auth/users') || [];
 387 |   renderUsers();
 388 | }
 389 | 
 390 | function renderUsers() {
 391 |   document.getElementById('users-count').textContent = allUsers.length;
 392 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('users-tbody');
 393 |   if (!allUsers.length) {
 394 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin usuarios</td></tr>`;
 395 |     return;
 396 |   }
 397 |   tbody.innerHTML = allUsers.map(u => `
 398 |     <tr>
 399 |       <td><strong>${u.username}</strong></td>
 400 |       <td><span class="role-badge role-${u.role}">${u.role}</span></td>
 401 |       <td>
 402 |         <span class="${u.is_active ? 'active-dot' : 'inactive-dot'}"></span>
 403 |         ${u.is_active ? 'Activo' : 'Inactivo'}
 404 |       </td>
 405 |       <td>
 406 |         <div class="action-btns">
 407 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="openPwdModal(${u.id}, '${u.username}')">
 408 |             <i class="fas fa-key"></i> Contraseña
 409 |           </button>
 410 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="toggleUser(${u.id})"
 411 |             style="${u.is_active ? 'background:#fef3c7;color:#92400e;' : 'background:#d1fae5;color:#065f46;'}">
 412 |             <i class="fas fa-${u.is_active ? 'ban' : 'check'}"></i>
 413 |             ${u.is_active ? 'Desactivar' : 'Activar'}
 414 |           </button>
 415 |           <button class="btn-del" onclick="deleteUser(${u.id}, '${u.username}')">
 416 |             <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
 417 |           </button>
 418 |         </div>
 419 |       </td>
 420 |     </tr>`).join('');
 421 | }
 422 | 
 423 | async function createUser() {
 424 |   const username = document.getElementById('new-username').value.trim();
 425 |   const password = document.getElementById('new-password').value;
 426 |   const role     = document.getElementById('new-role').value;
 427 |   if (!username || !password) { showToast('Completa usuario y contraseña', 'error'); return; }
 428 |   if (password.length < 6)    { showToast('La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres', 'error'); return; }
 429 |   const r = await apiRequest('/auth/users', 'POST', { username, password, role });
 430 |   if (r) {
 431 |     showToast(`Usuario ${username} creado`, 'success');
 432 |     document.getElementById('new-username').value = '';
 433 |     document.getElementById('new-password').value = '';
 434 |     loadUsers();
 435 |   }
 436 | }
 437 | 
 438 | async function toggleUser(id) {
 439 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/auth/users/${id}/toggle`, 'PATCH', {});
 440 |   if (r) { showToast(r.message); loadUsers(); }
 441 | }
 442 | 
 443 | async function deleteUser(id, username) {
 444 |   if (!confirm(`¿Eliminar el usuario "${username}"? Esta acción no se puede deshacer.`)) return;
 445 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/auth/users/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 446 |   if (r) { showToast('Usuario eliminado'); loadUsers(); }
 447 | }
 448 | 
 449 | function openPwdModal(id, username) {
 450 |   pwdTargetId = id;
 451 |   document.getElementById('pwd-modal-user').textContent = username;
 452 |   document.getElementById('modal-new-pwd').value = '';
 453 |   document.getElementById('pwd-modal').classList.add('open');
 454 | }
 455 | function closePwdModal() { document.getElementById('pwd-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
 456 | 
 457 | async function confirmPwdChange() {
 458 |   const pwd = document.getElementById('modal-new-pwd').value;
 459 |   if (!pwd || pwd.length < 6) { showToast('Mínimo 6 caracteres', 'error'); return; }
 460 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/auth/users/${pwdTargetId}/password`, 'PATCH', { new_password: pwd });
 461 |   if (r) { showToast('Contraseña actualizada'); closePwdModal(); }
 462 | }
 463 | 
 464 | // ════════════ PAGOS ═══════════════════════════════════════
 465 | 
 466 | async function loadPayments() {
 467 |   allPayments = await apiRequest('/finance/all-payments') || [];
 468 | 
 469 |   // Llenar selects de filtro
 470 |   const owners = [...new Set(allPayments.map(p => p.owner_name).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 471 |   const units  = [...new Set(allPayments.map(p => p.unit_number).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 472 |   const pfOwner = document.getElementById('pf-owner');
 473 |   const pfUnit  = document.getElementById('pf-unit');
 474 |   pfOwner.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 475 |   pfUnit.innerHTML  = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 476 |   owners.forEach(o => pfOwner.innerHTML += `<option>${o}</option>`);
 477 |   units.forEach(u  => pfUnit.innerHTML  += `<option value="${u}">Apt. ${u}</option>`);
 478 | 
 479 |   filterPayments();
 480 | }
 481 | 
 482 | function filterPayments() {
 483 |   const owner  = document.getElementById('pf-owner').value;
 484 |   const unit   = document.getElementById('pf-unit').value;
 485 |   const search = document.getElementById('pf-search').value.toLowerCase().trim();
 486 | 
 487 |   const list = allPayments.filter(p => {
 488 |     if (owner  && p.owner_name  !== owner) return false;
 489 |     if (unit   && p.unit_number !== unit)  return false;
 490 |     if (search) {
 491 |       const txt = [p.invoice_number, p.reference, p.owner_name, String(p.amount)].join(' ').toLowerCase();
 492 |       if (!txt.includes(search)) return false;
 493 |     }
 494 |     return true;
 495 |   });
 496 | 
 497 |   document.getElementById('payments-count').textContent = list.length;
 498 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('payments-tbody');
 499 | 
 500 |   if (!list.length) {
 501 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 502 |     return;
 503 |   }
 504 | 
 505 |   tbody.innerHTML = list.map(p => `
 506 |     <tr>
 507 |       <td class="td-mono" style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">#${p.payment_id}</td>
 508 |       <td>${formatDate(p.fecha)}</td>
 509 |       <td style="font-size:.83rem;">${p.owner_name}</td>
 510 |       <td>Apt. ${p.unit_number}</td>
 511 |       <td style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 512 |         ${p.cargos.map(c => `<div>${c.description} <strong>$${formatMoney(c.applied)}</strong></div>`).join('') || '—'}
 513 |       </td>
 514 |       <td class="td-right"><strong>$${formatMoney(p.amount)}</strong></td>
 515 |       <td style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">${p.invoice_number || '—'}</td>
 516 |       <td>
 517 |         <div class="action-btns">
 518 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="openEditPayment(${p.payment_id}, '${p.fecha}', ${p.amount}, '${p.invoice_number||''}', '${p.reference||''}')">
 519 |             <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Editar
 520 |           </button>
 521 |           <button class="btn-del" onclick="deletePayment(${p.payment_id})">
 522 |             <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
 523 |           </button>
 524 |         </div>
 525 |       </td>
 526 |     </tr>`).join('');
 527 | }
 528 | 
 529 | function clearPaymentFilters() {
 530 |   ['pf-owner','pf-unit','pf-search'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 531 |   filterPayments();
 532 | }
 533 | 
 534 | function openEditPayment(id, fecha, amount, invoice, ref) {
 535 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-id').value      = id;
 536 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-date').value    = fecha;
 537 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-amount').value  = amount;
 538 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-invoice').value = invoice;
 539 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-ref').value     = ref;
 540 |   document.getElementById('edit-payment-modal').classList.add('open');
 541 | }
 542 | function closeEditPayment() { document.getElementById('edit-payment-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
 543 | 
 544 | async function confirmEditPayment() {
 545 |   const id      = document.getElementById('edit-pay-id').value;
 546 |   const date    = document.getElementById('edit-pay-date').value;
 547 |   const amount  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-pay-amount').value);
 548 |   const invoice = document.getElementById('edit-pay-invoice').value.trim() || null;
 549 |   const ref     = document.getElementById('edit-pay-ref').value.trim()     || null;
 550 |   if (!date || !amount || amount <= 0) { showToast('Fecha y monto son obligatorios', 'error'); return; }
 551 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/finance/payment/${id}`, 'PUT', { payment_date: date, amount, invoice_number: invoice, reference: ref });
 552 |   if (r) { showToast('Pago actualizado'); closeEditPayment(); loadPayments(); }
 553 | }
 554 | 
 555 | async function deletePayment(id) {
 556 |   if (!confirm(`¿Eliminar el pago #${id}?\n\nEsto revertirá los saldos de los cargos vinculados.`)) return;
 557 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/finance/payment/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 558 |   if (r) { showToast('Pago eliminado y saldos revertidos', 'success'); loadPayments(); loadCharges(); }
 559 | }
 560 | 
 561 | // ════════════ CARGOS ══════════════════════════════════════
 562 | 
 563 | async function loadCharges() {
 564 |   allCharges = await apiRequest('/finance/charges') || [];
 565 | 
 566 |   const owners = [...new Set(allCharges.map(c => c.owner_name).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 567 |   const units  = [...new Set(allCharges.map(c => c.unit_number).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 568 |   const cfOwner = document.getElementById('cf-owner');
 569 |   const cfUnit  = document.getElementById('cf-unit');
 570 |   cfOwner.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 571 |   cfUnit.innerHTML  = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 572 |   owners.forEach(o => cfOwner.innerHTML += `<option>${o}</option>`);
 573 |   units.forEach(u  => cfUnit.innerHTML  += `<option value="${u}">Apt. ${u}</option>`);
 574 | 
 575 |   filterCharges();
 576 | }
 577 | 
 578 | function filterCharges() {
 579 |   const status = document.getElementById('cf-status').value;
 580 |   const owner  = document.getElementById('cf-owner').value;
 581 |   const unit   = document.getElementById('cf-unit').value;
 582 |   const desc   = document.getElementById('cf-desc').value.toLowerCase().trim();
 583 | 
 584 |   const list = allCharges.filter(c => {
 585 |     if (status && c.status      !== status) return false;
 586 |     if (owner  && c.owner_name  !== owner)  return false;
 587 |     if (unit   && c.unit_number !== unit)   return false;
 588 |     if (desc   && !c.description?.toLowerCase().includes(desc)) return false;
 589 |     return true;
 590 |   });
 591 | 
 592 |   document.getElementById('charges-count').textContent = list.length;
 593 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('charges-tbody');
 594 | 
 595 |   if (!list.length) {
 596 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 597 |     return;
 598 |   }
 599 | 
 600 |   tbody.innerHTML = list.map(c => `
 601 |     <tr>
 602 |       <td style="font-size:.83rem;">${c.owner_name || '<em style="color:var(--text-muted)">Sin asignar</em>'}</td>
 603 |       <td>${c.unit_number ? `Apt. ${c.unit_number}` : '—'}</td>
 604 |       <td><strong>${c.description}</strong></td>
 605 |       <td style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--text-secondary);">${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 606 |       <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.amount)}</td>
 607 |       <td class="td-right td-bold">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</td>
 608 |       <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 609 |       <td>
 610 |         <div class="action-btns">
 611 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="openEditCharge(${c.charge_id}, ${c.unit_id}, '${c.description}', ${c.amount}, '${c.date_created}', '${c.due_date}')">
 612 |             <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Editar
 613 |           </button>
 614 |           <button class="btn-del" onclick="deleteCharge(${c.charge_id}, '${c.description}')">
 615 |             <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
 616 |           </button>
 617 |         </div>
 618 |       </td>
 619 |     </tr>`).join('');
 620 | }
 621 | 
 622 | function clearChargeFilters() {
 623 |   ['cf-status','cf-owner','cf-unit','cf-desc'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 624 |   filterCharges();
 625 | }
 626 | 
 627 | function openEditCharge(id, unitId, desc, amount, dateCreated, dueDate) {
 628 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-id').value           = id;
 629 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-unit-id').value      = unitId;
 630 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-desc').value         = desc;
 631 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-amount').value       = amount;
 632 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-date-created').value = dateCreated;
 633 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-due-date').value     = dueDate;
 634 |   document.getElementById('edit-charge-modal').classList.add('open');
 635 | }
 636 | function closeEditCharge() { document.getElementById('edit-charge-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
 637 | 
 638 | async function confirmEditCharge() {
 639 |   const id          = document.getElementById('edit-chg-id').value;
 640 |   const unitId      = document.getElementById('edit-chg-unit-id').value;
 641 |   const desc        = document.getElementById('edit-chg-desc').value.trim();
 642 |   const amount      = parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-chg-amount').value);
 643 |   const dateCreated = document.getElementById('edit-chg-date-created').value;
 644 |   const dueDate     = document.getElementById('edit-chg-due-date').value;
 645 |   if (!desc || !amount || !dateCreated || !dueDate) { showToast('Completa todos los campos', 'error'); return; }
 646 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/charges/${id}`, 'PUT', {
 647 |     unit_id: parseInt(unitId), description: desc, amount, date_created: dateCreated, due_date: dueDate
 648 |   });
 649 |   if (r) { showToast('Cargo actualizado'); closeEditCharge(); loadCharges(); }
 650 | }
 651 | 
 652 | async function deleteCharge(id, desc) {
 653 |   if (!confirm(`¿Eliminar el cargo "${desc}"?\n\nEsto eliminará también los registros de pago vinculados a este cargo.`)) return;
 654 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/charges/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 655 |   if (r) { showToast('Cargo eliminado', 'success'); loadCharges(); loadPayments(); }
 656 | }
 657 | 
 658 | // Cerrar modales al click fuera
 659 | ['pwd-modal','edit-payment-modal','edit-charge-modal'].forEach(id => {
 660 |   document.getElementById(id).addEventListener('click', function(e) {
 661 |     if (e.target === this) this.classList.remove('open');
 662 |   });
 663 | });
 664 | </script>
 665 | </body>
 666 | </html>

 251 | <div id="notification"></div>
 252 | <script src="js/main.js"></script>
 253 | <script>
 254 | renderHeader('agenda');
 255 | 
 256 | let allEvents  = [];
 257 | let evEditingId = null;
 258 | let calYear, calMonth;
 259 | let activeFilter = 'ALL';
 260 | 
 261 | const TYPE_ICONS = { CITA:'fa-handshake', EVENTO:'fa-landmark', TAREA:'fa-check-square' };
 262 | 
 263 | // ── Init ─────────────────────────────────────
 264 | async function init() {
 265 |   const now = new Date();
 266 |   calYear  = now.getFullYear();
 267 |   calMonth = now.getMonth();
 268 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value = todayISO();
 269 |   await loadEvents();
 270 | }
 271 | 
 272 | // ── Tabs ──────────────────────────────────────
 273 | function switchTab(tab) {
 274 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ag-tab').forEach((b,i) => {
 275 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['calendario','lista','nuevo'][i] === tab);
 276 |   });
 277 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ag-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 278 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 279 | }
 280 | 
 281 | // ── Cargar eventos ────────────────────────────
 282 | async function loadEvents() {
 283 |   allEvents = await apiRequest('/agenda') || [];
 284 |   renderCalendar();
 285 |   renderList();
 286 | }
 287 | 
 288 | // ── Filtro lista ──────────────────────────────
 289 | function setFilter(f, el) {
 290 |   activeFilter = f;
 291 |   document.querySelectorAll('.filter-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('on'));
 292 |   el.classList.add('on');
 293 |   renderList();
 294 | }
 295 | 
 296 | function renderList() {
 297 |   let list = allEvents;
 298 |   if (activeFilter !== 'ALL') {
 299 |     if (['CITA','EVENTO','TAREA'].includes(activeFilter))
 300 |       list = list.filter(e => e.event_type === activeFilter);
 301 |     else
 302 |       list = list.filter(e => e.status === activeFilter);
 303 |   }
 304 | 
 305 |   document.getElementById('ev-count').textContent = list.length;
 306 |   const container = document.getElementById('ev-list');
 307 | 
 308 |   if (!list.length) {
 309 |     container.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 310 |       <i class="fas fa-calendar-times" style="font-size:2rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 311 |       Sin eventos que mostrar</div>`;
 312 |     return;
 313 |   }
 314 | 
 315 |   // Agrupar por fecha
 316 |   const grouped = {};
 317 |   list.forEach(e => {
 318 |     const key = e.event_date;
 319 |     if (!grouped[key]) grouped[key] = [];
 320 |     grouped[key].push(e);
 321 |   });
 322 | 
 323 |   container.innerHTML = Object.keys(grouped).sort().map(dateKey => {
 324 |     const d = new Date(dateKey + 'T00:00:00');
 325 |     const label = d.toLocaleDateString('es-PA', { weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' });
 326 |     return `
 327 |       <div style="font-size:.72rem;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;
 328 |         color:var(--text-muted);padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);margin:12px 0 8px;">
 329 |         ${label}
 330 |       </div>
 331 |       ${grouped[dateKey].map(e => `
 332 |         <div class="event-card priority-${e.priority}">
 333 |           <div class="event-type-icon icon-${e.event_type}">
 334 |             <i class="fas ${TYPE_ICONS[e.event_type]}"></i>
 335 |           </div>
 336 |           <div class="event-info">
 337 |             <strong>${e.title}</strong>
 338 |             <div class="event-meta">
 339 |               ${e.event_time ? `<i class="fas fa-clock" style="opacity:.5;"></i> ${e.event_time} &nbsp;` : ''}
 340 |               ${e.location ? `<i class="fas fa-map-marker-alt" style="opacity:.5;"></i> ${e.location} &nbsp;` : ''}
 341 |               ${e.description ? `<span style="opacity:.7;">${e.description}</span>` : ''}
 342 |             </div>
 343 |           </div>
 344 |           <div class="event-actions">
 345 |             <span class="status-chip chip-${e.status}">${e.status}</span>
 346 |             ${e.status === 'PENDIENTE' ? `
 347 |               <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" title="Marcar completado"
 348 |                 onclick="markDone(${e.id})" style="color:var(--success);">
 349 |                 <i class="fas fa-check"></i>
 350 |               </button>` : ''}
 351 |             <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="editEvent(${e.id})" title="Editar">
 352 |               <i class="fas fa-pencil-alt"></i>
 353 |             </button>
 354 |             <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="deleteEvent(${e.id})" title="Eliminar">
 355 |               <i class="fas fa-trash" style="color:var(--danger);"></i>
 356 |             </button>
 357 |           </div>
 358 |         </div>`).join('')}`;
 359 |   }).join('');
 360 | }
 361 | 
 362 | // ── Calendario ────────────────────────────────
 363 | function prevMonth() { if (--calMonth < 0) { calMonth = 11; calYear--; } renderCalendar(); }
 364 | function nextMonth() { if (++calMonth > 11) { calMonth = 0;  calYear++; } renderCalendar(); }
 365 | 
 366 | function renderCalendar() {
 367 |   const months = ['Enero','Febrero','Marzo','Abril','Mayo','Junio',
 368 |                   'Julio','Agosto','Septiembre','Octubre','Noviembre','Diciembre'];
 369 |   document.getElementById('cal-title').textContent = `${months[calMonth]} ${calYear}`;
 370 | 
 371 |   const firstDay = new Date(calYear, calMonth, 1).getDay();
 372 |   const daysInMonth = new Date(calYear, calMonth + 1, 0).getDate();
 373 |   const daysInPrev  = new Date(calYear, calMonth, 0).getDate();
 374 |   const today = todayISO();
 375 | 
 376 |   // Indexar eventos del mes
 377 |   const evMap = {};
 378 |   allEvents.forEach(e => {
 379 |     const [y, m] = e.event_date.split('-').map(Number);
 380 |     if (y === calYear && m - 1 === calMonth) {
 381 |       const d = parseInt(e.event_date.split('-')[2]);
 382 |       if (!evMap[d]) evMap[d] = [];
 383 |       evMap[d].push(e);
 384 |     }
 385 |   });
 386 | 
 387 |   let html = '';
 388 |   let day = 1;
 389 | 
 390 |   // Días del mes anterior
 391 |   for (let i = 0; i < firstDay; i++) {
 392 |     html += `<div class="cal-day other-month">
 393 |       <div class="day-num">${daysInPrev - firstDay + i + 1}</div></div>`;
 394 |   }
 395 |   // Días del mes actual
 396 |   for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
 397 |     const dateStr = `${calYear}-${String(calMonth+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(d).padStart(2,'0')}`;
 398 |     const isToday = dateStr === today;
 399 |     const evs = evMap[d] || [];
 400 |     html += `<div class="cal-day${isToday ? ' today' : ''}" onclick="openDayModal('${dateStr}')">
 401 |       <div class="day-num">${isToday ? `<span style="background:var(--accent);color:#fff;width:22px;height:22px;border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;">${d}</span>` : d}</div>
 402 |       <div class="day-events">
 403 |         ${evs.slice(0, 3).map(e => `
 404 |           <div class="day-event-dot dot-${e.event_type} ${e.status!=='PENDIENTE'?'dot-done':''}"
 405 |             onclick="event.stopPropagation();editEvent(${e.id})">
 406 |             ${e.title}
 407 |           </div>`).join('')}
 408 |         ${evs.length > 3 ? `<div style="font-size:.65rem;color:var(--text-muted);padding:0 2px;">+${evs.length-3} más</div>` : ''}
 409 |       </div>
 410 |     </div>`;
 411 |   }
 412 |   // Días del mes siguiente
 413 |   const remaining = 42 - firstDay - daysInMonth;
 414 |   for (let i = 1; i <= remaining; i++) {
 415 |     html += `<div class="cal-day other-month"><div class="day-num">${i}</div></div>`;
 416 |   }
 417 | 
 418 |   document.getElementById('cal-grid').innerHTML = html;
 419 | }
 420 | 
 421 | function openDayModal(dateStr) {
 422 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value = dateStr;
 423 |   switchTab('nuevo');
 424 | }
 425 | 
 426 | // ── Guardar evento ────────────────────────────
 427 | async function saveEvent() {
 428 |   const title = document.getElementById('ev-title').value.trim();
 429 |   const dt    = document.getElementById('ev-date').value;
 430 |   if (!title || !dt) { showToast('Título y fecha son obligatorios', 'error'); return; }
 431 | 
 432 |   const time = document.getElementById('ev-time').value;
 433 |   const data = {
 434 |     title,
 435 |     description: document.getElementById('ev-desc').value.trim()     || null,
 436 |     event_type:  document.getElementById('ev-type').value,
 437 |     event_date:  dt,
 438 |     event_time:  time || null,
 439 |     location:    document.getElementById('ev-location').value.trim() || null,
 440 |     priority:    document.getElementById('ev-priority').value,
 441 |     status:      document.getElementById('ev-status').value,
 442 |   };
 443 | 
 444 |   let r;
 445 |   if (evEditingId) {
 446 |     r = await apiRequest(`/agenda/${evEditingId}`, 'PUT', data);
 447 |     if (r) showToast('Evento actualizado');
 448 |   } else {
 449 |     r = await apiRequest('/agenda/', 'POST', data);
 450 |     if (r) showToast('Evento guardado');
 451 |   }
 452 |   if (r) { cancelEvEdit(); loadEvents(); switchTab('calendario'); }
 453 | }
 454 | 
 455 | function editEvent(id) {
 456 |   const e = allEvents.find(x => x.id === id);
 457 |   if (!e) return;
 458 |   evEditingId = id;
 459 |   document.getElementById('ev-id').value            = id;
 460 |   document.getElementById('ev-type').value          = e.event_type;
 461 |   document.getElementById('ev-title').value         = e.title;
 462 |   document.getElementById('ev-desc').value          = e.description || '';
 463 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value          = e.event_date;
 464 |   document.getElementById('ev-time').value          = e.event_time || '';
 465 |   document.getElementById('ev-location').value      = e.location || '';
 466 |   document.getElementById('ev-priority').value      = e.priority;
 467 |   document.getElementById('ev-status').value        = e.status;
 468 |   document.getElementById('ev-form-title').textContent = 'Editar Evento';
 469 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-label').textContent  = 'Actualizar';
 470 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-cancel').style.display = '';
 471 |   switchTab('nuevo');
 472 | }
 473 | 
 474 | function cancelEvEdit() {
 475 |   evEditingId = null;
 476 |   ['ev-id','ev-title','ev-desc','ev-time','ev-location'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 477 |   document.getElementById('ev-type').value     = 'CITA';
 478 |   document.getElementById('ev-priority').value = 'NORMAL';
 479 |   document.getElementById('ev-status').value   = 'PENDIENTE';
 480 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value     = todayISO();
 481 |   document.getElementById('ev-form-title').textContent = 'Nuevo Evento';
 482 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-label').textContent  = 'Guardar Evento';
 483 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-cancel').style.display = 'none';
 484 | }
 485 | 
 486 | async function markDone(id) {
 487 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/agenda/${id}/status?status=COMPLETADO`, 'PATCH');
 488 |   if (r) { showToast('Marcado como completado', 'success'); loadEvents(); }
 489 | }
 490 | 
 491 | async function deleteEvent(id) {
 492 |   if (!confirm('¿Eliminar este evento?')) return;
 493 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/agenda/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 494 |   if (r) { showToast('Evento eliminado'); loadEvents(); }
 495 | }
 496 | 
 497 | init();
 498 | </script>
 499 | </body>
 500 | </html>
 501 |

 255 | <script>
 256 | const fmoney = v => parseFloat(v||0).toLocaleString('es-PA', { minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2 });
 257 | const fdate  = s => {
 258 |   if (!s) return '—';
 259 |   try {
 260 |     const [y,m,d] = s.split('T')[0].split('-');
 261 |     const months = ['ene','feb','mar','abr','may','jun','jul','ago','sep','oct','nov','dic'];
 262 |     return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;
 263 |   } catch { return s; }
 264 | };
 265 | 
 266 | (async () => {
 267 |   const params  = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
 268 |   const ownerId = params.get('owner_id');
 269 |   if (!ownerId) { document.getElementById('loading').textContent = 'No se especificó un propietario.'; return; }
 270 | 
 271 |   try {
 272 |     const token   = localStorage.getItem('access_token');
 273 |     const headers = token ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 274 | 
 275 |     const data = await fetch(`/api/finance/owner-statement-detailed/${ownerId}`, { headers })
 276 |       .then(r => { if (!r.ok) throw new Error('No encontrado'); return r.json(); });
 277 | 
 278 |     const logoEl = document.getElementById('stmt-logo');
 279 |     const img    = new Image();
 280 |     img.onload   = () => { logoEl.innerHTML = `<img src="/static/logo.png" alt="Logo">`; };
 281 |     img.src      = '/static/logo.png';
 282 | 
 283 |     const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', { year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' });
 284 | 
 285 |     document.getElementById('stmt-date').textContent      = today;
 286 |     document.getElementById('gen-date').textContent       = today;
 287 |     document.getElementById('s-owner').textContent        = data.owner_name    || '—';
 288 |     document.getElementById('s-unit').textContent         = data.unit_number   ? `Apt. ${data.unit_number}` : '—';
 289 |     document.getElementById('s-prop').textContent         = data.property_name || '—';
 290 |     document.getElementById('stmt-prop-addr').textContent = data.property_address || 'Administración de Propiedades';
 291 | 
 292 |     const stmt = data.statement || [];
 293 |     let tFact = 0, tPaid = 0, tPend = 0;
 294 |     stmt.forEach(c => { tFact += c.amount||0; tPaid += c.paid||0; tPend += c.balance||0; });
 295 | 
 296 |     document.getElementById('sum-total').textContent = `$${fmoney(tFact)}`;
 297 |     document.getElementById('sum-paid').textContent  = `$${fmoney(tPaid)}`;
 298 |     document.getElementById('sum-pend').textContent  = `$${fmoney(tPend)}`;
 299 | 
 300 |     const tbody = document.getElementById('stmt-tbody');
 301 | 
 302 |     if (!stmt.length) {
 303 |       tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#bbb;">Sin cargos registrados</td></tr>`;
 304 |     } else {
 305 |       stmt.forEach(c => {
 306 |         tbody.innerHTML += `
 307 |           <tr>
 308 |             <td class="b">${c.description}</td>
 309 |             <td class="muted">${fdate(c.due_date)}</td>
 310 |             <td class="r">$${fmoney(c.amount)}</td>
 311 |             <td class="r">$${fmoney(c.paid)}</td>
 312 |             <td class="r b" style="color:${c.balance>0?'#c0392b':'#27ae60'}">$${fmoney(c.balance)}</td>
 313 |             <td><span class="st st-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 314 |           </tr>`;
 315 | 
 316 |         if (c.payments?.length) {
 317 |           tbody.innerHTML += `<tr class="pay-detail-row">
 318 |             <td colspan="6">
 319 |               <div class="pay-detail-inner">
 320 |                 ${c.payments.map(p => `
 321 |                   <span>✓ <strong>$${fmoney(p.applied_amount)}</strong></span>
 322 |                   <span>${fdate(p.payment_date)}</span>
 323 |                   ${p.fiscal_invoice_number ? `<span>Factura: ${p.fiscal_invoice_number}</span>` : ''}
 324 |                 `).join(' &nbsp;·&nbsp; ')}
 325 |               </div>
 326 |             </td>
 327 |           </tr>`;
 328 |         }
 329 |       });
 330 |     }
 331 | 
 332 |     document.getElementById('loading').style.display   = 'none';
 333 |     document.getElementById('stmt-page').style.display = 'block';
 334 | 
 335 |   } catch(e) {
 336 |     document.getElementById('loading').textContent = `Error: ${e.message}`;
 337 |   }
 338 | })();
 339 | </script>
 340 | </body>
 341 | </html>

 226 | <script>
 227 | const fmoney = v => parseFloat(v||0).toLocaleString('es-PA', {
 228 |   minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2
 229 | });
 230 | const fdate = s => {
 231 |   if (!s) return '—';
 232 |   try {
 233 |     const [y,m,d] = String(s).split('T')[0].split('-');
 234 |     const months = ['ene','feb','mar','abr','may','jun','jul','ago','sep','oct','nov','dic'];
 235 |     return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;
 236 |   } catch { return s; }
 237 | };
 238 | 
 239 | (async () => {
 240 |   const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
 241 |   const pid    = params.get('payment_id');
 242 |   if (!pid) { document.getElementById('loading').textContent = 'No se especificó un pago.'; return; }
 243 | 
 244 |   try {
 245 |     const token   = localStorage.getItem('access_token');
 246 |     const headers = token ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 247 | 
 248 |     const [pay, detail] = await Promise.all([
 249 |       fetch(`/api/finance/payment/${pid}`,             { headers }).then(r => r.json()),
 250 |       fetch(`/api/finance/payment-detail-full/${pid}`, { headers }).then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null),
 251 |     ]);
 252 | 
 253 |     // Logo
 254 |     const logoEl = document.getElementById('inv-logo');
 255 |     const img    = new Image();
 256 |     img.onload   = () => { logoEl.innerHTML = `<img src="/static/logo.png" alt="Logo">`; };
 257 |     img.src      = '/static/logo.png';
 258 | 
 259 |     const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', {
 260 |       year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'
 261 |     });
 262 | 
 263 |     // Referencia
 264 |     let refHtml = '';
 265 |     if (detail?.invoice_number)       refHtml += `N° Sistema: ${detail.invoice_number}<br>`;
 266 |     if (detail?.fiscal_invoice_number) refHtml += `N° Fiscal: ${detail.fiscal_invoice_number}`;
 267 |     document.getElementById('inv-ref-num').innerHTML = refHtml || `Pago #${pid}`;
 268 | 
 269 |     // Propietario
 270 |     document.getElementById('inv-owner').innerHTML =
 271 |       `${detail?.owner_name || '—'}
 272 |        <small>Unidad: ${detail?.unit_number || '—'}</small>
 273 |        <small>Propiedad: ${detail?.property_name || '—'}</small>`;
 274 | 
 275 |     // Datos del pago
 276 |     document.getElementById('inv-pay-info').innerHTML =
 277 |       `Fecha: ${fdate(detail?.payment_date || pay?.payment_date)}
 278 |        ${detail?.reference ? `<small>Referencia: ${detail.reference}</small>` : ''}`;
 279 | 
 280 |     // Tabla de cargos
 281 |     const tbody = document.getElementById('inv-tbody');
 282 |     const apps  = pay?.applications || [];
 283 | 
 284 |     if (!apps.length) {
 285 |       tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;padding:16px;color:#bbb;">Sin detalle disponible</td></tr>`;
 286 |     } else {
 287 |       apps.forEach((a, i) => {
 288 |         tbody.innerHTML += `
 289 |           <tr>
 290 |             <td class="muted">${i+1}</td>
 291 |             <td>${a.description || `Cargo #${a.charge_id}`}</td>
 292 |             <td class="r">$${fmoney(a.applied_amount)}</td>
 293 |           </tr>`;
 294 |       });
 295 |     }
 296 | 
 297 |     document.getElementById('inv-total').textContent = `$${fmoney(pay?.amount || 0)}`;
 298 |     document.getElementById('inv-date').textContent  = today;
 299 | 
 300 |     document.getElementById('loading').style.display  = 'none';
 301 |     document.getElementById('inv-page').style.display = 'block';
 302 | 
 303 |   } catch(e) {
 304 |     document.getElementById('loading').textContent = `Error: ${e.message}`;
 305 |   }
 306 | })();

 444 | <div id="notification"></div>
 445 | <script src="js/main.js"></script>
 446 | <script>
 447 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 448 | // ESTADO GLOBAL
 449 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 450 | let mode          = 'owner';
 451 | let activeOwnerId = null;
 452 | let lastPaymentId = null;
 453 | let allChargesCache = [];
 454 | let allPropsCache   = [];
 455 | let allUnitsCache   = [];
 456 | 
 457 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 458 | // INIT
 459 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 460 | async function init() {
 461 |   
 462 | 
 463 |   const [props, owners, units] = await Promise.all([
 464 |     apiRequest('/properties'),
 465 |     apiRequest('/owners'),
 466 |     apiRequest('/units'),
 467 |   ]);
 468 | 
 469 |   allPropsCache = props  || [];
 470 |   allUnitsCache = units  || [];
 471 | 
 472 |   // Owner select (pago)
 473 |   const ownerSel = document.getElementById('owner-select');
 474 |   (owners || []).forEach(o =>
 475 |     ownerSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 476 |   ownerSel.addEventListener('change', () => {
 477 |     const id = parseInt(ownerSel.value);
 478 |     if (!id) { resetPayForm(); return; }
 479 |     activeOwnerId = id;
 480 |     document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'none';
 481 |     loadOwnerCharges(id);
 482 |   });
 483 | 
 484 |   // Prop select (pago por unidad)
 485 |   const propPaySel = document.getElementById('prop-pay-select');
 486 |   allPropsCache.forEach(p =>
 487 |     propPaySel.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 488 | 
 489 |   // Prop select (cargo)
 490 |   const chargePropSel = document.getElementById('charge-prop-select');
 491 |   allPropsCache.forEach(p =>
 492 |     chargePropSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 493 | 
 494 |   // Estado de cuenta select
 495 |   const stmtSel = document.getElementById('stmt-select');
 496 |   (owners || []).forEach(o =>
 497 |     stmtSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 498 | 
 499 |   // Fechas por defecto
 500 |   document.getElementById('charge-date').value = todayISO();
 501 | 
 502 |   // Cargar historial
 503 |   await loadChargesTable();
 504 | }
 505 | 
 506 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 507 | // TABS
 508 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 509 | function switchTab(tab) {
 510 |   document.querySelectorAll('.fin-tab').forEach((b, i) => {
 511 |     const ids = ['pagos','cargos','historial','estados'];
 512 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ids[i] === tab);
 513 |   });
 514 |   document.querySelectorAll('.fin-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 515 |   document.getElementById(`panel-${tab}`).classList.add('active');
 516 | 
 517 |   if (tab === 'historial') loadChargesTable();
 518 | }
 519 | 
 520 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 521 | // TOGGLE MODO PAGO
 522 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 523 | function switchMode(m) {
 524 |   mode = m;
 525 |   activeOwnerId = null;
 526 |   document.getElementById('btn-owner').classList.toggle('active', m === 'owner');
 527 |   document.getElementById('btn-unit').classList.toggle('active',  m === 'unit');
 528 |   document.getElementById('panel-owner').style.display = m === 'owner' ? '' : 'none';
 529 |   document.getElementById('panel-unit').style.display  = m === 'unit'  ? '' : 'none';
 530 |   document.getElementById('owner-select').value = '';
 531 |   document.getElementById('prop-pay-select').value = '';
 532 |   resetPayForm();
 533 | }
 534 | 
 535 | function resetPayForm() {
 536 |   activeOwnerId = null;
 537 |   lastPaymentId = null;
 538 |   document.getElementById('owner-info-box').style.display = 'none';
 539 |   document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'none';
 540 |   document.getElementById('charges-panel').innerHTML = `
 541 |     <div class="charges-empty">
 542 |       <i class="fas fa-hand-point-up"></i>
 543 |       Selecciona un propietario o apartamento
 544 |     </div>`;
 545 |   document.getElementById('payment-form-wrapper').innerHTML = `
 546 |     <div class="charges-empty" style="padding:2.5rem 1rem;">
 547 |       <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i>
 548 |       Selecciona los cargos a pagar primero
 549 |     </div>`;
 550 | }
 551 | 
 552 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 553 | // CARGAR UNIDADES POR PROPIEDAD (modo unidad)
 554 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 555 | function loadUnitsByProp() {
 556 |   const propId = parseInt(document.getElementById('prop-pay-select').value);
 557 |   const sel = document.getElementById('unit-pay-select');
 558 |   sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione unidad</option>';
 559 |   const filtered = propId ? allUnitsCache.filter(u => u.property_id === propId) : allUnitsCache;
 560 |   filtered.forEach(u => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`);
 561 |   resetPayForm();
 562 | }
 563 | 
 564 | async function loadUnitCharges() {
 565 |   const unitId = parseInt(document.getElementById('unit-pay-select').value);
 566 |   if (!unitId) { resetPayForm(); return; }
 567 | 
 568 |   const data = await apiRequest(`/finance/unit-statement/${unitId}`);
 569 |   if (!data) return;
 570 | 
 571 |   activeOwnerId = data.owner_id;
 572 |   document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'none';
 573 | 
 574 |   const infoBox = document.getElementById('owner-info-box');
 575 |   if (data.owner_id) {
 576 |     infoBox.style.display = 'block';
 577 |     document.getElementById('owner-info-text').textContent =
 578 |       `Propietario activo: ${data.owner_name}`;
 579 |   } else {
 580 |     infoBox.style.display = 'block';
 581 |     document.getElementById('owner-info-text').textContent =
 582 |       '⚠ Esta unidad no tiene propietario activo asignado.';
 583 |   }
 584 | 
 585 |   renderCharges(data.charges || []);
 586 | }
 587 | 
 588 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 589 | // CARGOS DEL PROPIETARIO
 590 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 591 | async function loadOwnerCharges(ownerId) {
 592 |   const charges = await apiRequest(`/finance/owner-statement/${ownerId}`);
 593 |   renderCharges(charges || []);
 594 | }
 595 | 
 596 | function renderCharges(charges) {
 597 |   const panel = document.getElementById('charges-panel');
 598 |   const formW = document.getElementById('payment-form-wrapper');
 599 | 
 600 |   const pendientes = charges.filter(c => c.status !== 'PAGADO');
 601 | 
 602 |   if (!pendientes.length) {
 603 |     panel.innerHTML = `
 604 |       <div class="charges-empty">
 605 |         <i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:var(--success)"></i>
 606 |         Sin cargos pendientes
 607 |       </div>`;
 608 |     formW.innerHTML = `
 609 |       <div class="charges-empty" style="padding:2.5rem 1rem;">
 610 |         <i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:var(--success)"></i>
 611 |         Este propietario no tiene deuda pendiente
 612 |       </div>`;
 613 |     return;
 614 |   }
 615 | 
 616 |   // Renderizar lista de cargos
 617 |   let html = `<p style="font-weight:600;font-size:.85rem;margin-bottom:10px;color:var(--text-secondary);">
 618 |     Selecciona los cargos a incluir en el pago:</p>`;
 619 | 
 620 |   pendientes.forEach(c => {
 621 |     html += `
 622 |     <div class="charge-row">
 623 |       <input type="checkbox" id="chk-${c.charge_id}" value="${c.charge_id}" onchange="recalcTotal()">
 624 |       <label for="chk-${c.charge_id}">
 625 |         <span class="cdesc">${c.description}</span>
 626 |         <span class="cmeta">Vence: ${formatDate(c.due_date)} &nbsp;·&nbsp;
 627 |           Total: $${formatMoney(c.total || c.amount)} &nbsp;·&nbsp;
 628 |           <strong>Saldo: $${formatMoney(c.balance)}</strong></span>
 629 |       </label>
 630 |       <span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span>
 631 |       <input type="number"
 632 |              data-charge="${c.charge_id}"
 633 |              data-max="${parseFloat(c.balance).toFixed(4)}"
 634 |              value="${parseFloat(c.balance).toFixed(2)}"
 635 |              step="0.01" min="0.01" max="${parseFloat(c.balance).toFixed(2)}"
 636 |              style="width:110px;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"
 637 |              oninput="recalcTotal()">
 638 |     </div>`;
 639 |   });
 640 | 
 641 |   panel.innerHTML = html;
 642 | 
 643 |   // Renderizar formulario de pago
 644 |   formW.innerHTML = `
 645 |     <label class="field-label">Total calculado</label>
 646 |     <div class="total-preview">
 647 |       <span>Monto a registrar</span>
 648 |       <strong id="total-display">$0.00</strong>
 649 |     </div>
 650 | 
 651 |     <label class="field-label">Fecha de pago</label>
 652 |     <input type="date" id="pay-date" value="${todayISO()}">
 653 | 
 654 |     <label class="field-label">N° Factura física (opcional)</label>
 655 |     <input type="text" id="pay-invoice" placeholder="Ej: 00542">
 656 | 
 657 |     <label class="field-label">Referencia / N° Transferencia (opcional)</label>
 658 |     <input type="text" id="pay-ref" placeholder="Ej: T-0098345">
 659 | 
 660 |     <div id="pay-feedback"></div>
 661 | 
 662 |     <button onclick="registerPayment()" style="width:100%;justify-content:center;margin-top:6px;">
 663 |       <i class="fas fa-save"></i> Registrar Pago
 664 |     </button>`;
 665 | 
 666 |   recalcTotal();
 667 | }
 668 | 
 669 | function recalcTotal() {
 670 |   let total = 0;
 671 |   document.querySelectorAll('#charges-panel input[type=checkbox]:checked').forEach(cb => {
 672 |     const inp = document.querySelector(`input[data-charge='${cb.value}']`);
 673 |     if (inp) total += parseFloat(inp.value) || 0;
 674 |   });
 675 |   const el = document.getElementById('total-display');
 676 |   if (el) el.textContent = `$${formatMoney(total)}`;
 677 | }
 678 | 
 679 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 680 | // REGISTRAR PAGO
 681 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 682 | async function registerPayment() {
 683 |   const fb = document.getElementById('pay-feedback');
 684 |   if (fb) fb.innerHTML = '';
 685 | 
 686 |   if (!activeOwnerId) {
 687 |     showToast('No hay propietario seleccionado', 'error'); return;
 688 |   }
 689 | 
 690 |   const applications = [];
 691 |   let error = null;
 692 | 
 693 |   document.querySelectorAll('#charges-panel input[type=checkbox]:checked').forEach(cb => {
 694 |     if (error) return;
 695 |     const chargeId = parseInt(cb.value);
 696 |     const inp      = document.querySelector(`input[data-charge='${chargeId}']`);
 697 |     const max      = parseFloat(inp.dataset.max);
 698 |     const amount   = parseFloat(inp.value);
 699 | 
 700 |     if (!amount || amount <= 0) { error = 'El monto debe ser mayor a $0.00'; return; }
 701 |     if (amount > max + 0.005)   { error = `$${amount.toFixed(2)} supera el saldo ($${max.toFixed(2)})`; return; }
 702 |     applications.push({ charge_id: chargeId, amount: parseFloat(amount.toFixed(2)) });
 703 |   });
 704 | 
 705 |   if (error) {
 706 |     if (fb) fb.innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-error">${error}</div>`; return;
 707 |   }
 708 |   if (!applications.length) {
 709 |     if (fb) fb.innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-warning">Selecciona al menos un cargo</div>`; return;
 710 |   }
 711 | 
 712 |   const payDate = document.getElementById('pay-date')?.value;
 713 |   if (!payDate) {
 714 |     if (fb) fb.innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-error">Ingresa la fecha del pago</div>`; return;
 715 |   }
 716 | 
 717 |   const total = applications.reduce((s, a) => s + a.amount, 0);
 718 | 
 719 |   const result = await apiRequest('/finance/payment-complete', 'POST', {
 720 |     owner_id:       activeOwnerId,
 721 |     payment_date:   payDate,
 722 |     amount:         parseFloat(total.toFixed(2)),
 723 |     invoice_number: document.getElementById('pay-invoice')?.value || null,
 724 |     reference:      document.getElementById('pay-ref')?.value     || null,
 725 |     applications,
 726 |   });
 727 | 
 728 |   if (result) {
 729 |     lastPaymentId = result.payment_id;
 730 |     document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'block';
 731 |     document.getElementById('pay-feedback').innerHTML =
 732 |       `<div class="alert alert-success">✓ Pago #${lastPaymentId} registrado correctamente</div>`;
 733 | 
 734 |     await loadChargesTable();
 735 | 
 736 |     // Refrescar cargos
 737 |     if (mode === 'owner') {
 738 |       loadOwnerCharges(activeOwnerId);
 739 |     } else {
 740 |       const uid = parseInt(document.getElementById('unit-pay-select').value);
 741 |       if (uid) loadUnitCharges(uid);
 742 |     }
 743 |   }
 744 | }
 745 | 
 746 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 747 | // FACTURA
 748 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 749 | function openInvoiceModal() {
 750 |   document.getElementById('modal-fiscal').value = '';
 751 |   document.getElementById('invoice-modal').classList.add('open');
 752 | }
 753 | 
 754 | function closeInvoiceModal() {
 755 |   document.getElementById('invoice-modal').classList.remove('open');
 756 | }

 758 | async function confirmInvoice() {
 759 |   closeInvoiceModal();
 760 |   if (!lastPaymentId) return;
 761 |   const fiscal = document.getElementById('modal-fiscal').value.trim();
 762 |   if (fiscal) {
 763 |     await apiRequest(`/finance/generate-invoice/payment/${lastPaymentId}?fiscal_number=${encodeURIComponent(fiscal)}`, 'POST');
 764 |   }
 765 |   window.open(`/static/factura.html?payment_id=${lastPaymentId}`, '_blank');
 766 | }
 767 | 
 768 | function openStatementFromPay() {
 769 |   if (!activeOwnerId) return;
 770 |   window.open(`/static/estado_cuenta.html?owner_id=${activeOwnerId}&t=${Date.now()}`, '_blank');
 771 | }
 772 | 
 773 | function openStatementSelected() {
 774 |   const id = document.getElementById('stmt-select').value;
 775 |   if (!id) { showToast('Selecciona un propietario', 'warning'); return; }
 776 |   window.open(`/static/estado_cuenta.html?owner_id=${id}&t=${Date.now()}`, '_blank');
 777 | }

 779 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 780 | // CREAR CARGO
 781 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 782 | function loadChargeUnits() {
 783 |   const propId = parseInt(document.getElementById('charge-prop-select').value);
 784 |   const sel = document.getElementById('charge-unit-select');
 785 |   sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todas las unidades</option>';
 786 | 
 787 |   const units = propId ? allUnitsCache.filter(u => u.property_id === propId) : allUnitsCache;
 788 |   units.forEach(u => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`);
 789 | 
 790 |   // Preview unidades afectadas
 791 |   const preview = document.getElementById('affected-units');
 792 |   if (!propId) {
 793 |     preview.innerHTML = `<div class="charges-empty"><i class="fas fa-building"></i>Selecciona una propiedad</div>`;
 794 |     return;
 795 |   }
 796 | 
 797 |   if (!units.length) {
 798 |     preview.innerHTML = `<div class="charges-empty"><i class="fas fa-info-circle"></i>Sin unidades en esta propiedad</div>`;
 799 |     return;
 800 |   }
 801 | 
 802 |   preview.innerHTML = `
 803 |     <p style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--text-secondary);margin-bottom:10px;">
 804 |       Si no seleccionas unidad específica, el cargo se creará para estas ${units.length} unidades:
 805 |     </p>
 806 |     <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:6px;">
 807 |       ${units.map(u => `<span class="badge badge-primary">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</span>`).join('')}
 808 |     </div>`;
 809 | }
 810 | 
 811 | async function createCharge() {
 812 |   const propId  = parseInt(document.getElementById('charge-prop-select').value);
 813 |   const unitId  = parseInt(document.getElementById('charge-unit-select').value) || null;
 814 |   const desc    = document.getElementById('charge-desc').value.trim();
 815 |   const amount  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('charge-amount').value);
 816 |   const created = document.getElementById('charge-date').value;
 817 |   const due     = document.getElementById('charge-due').value;
 818 | 
 819 |   if (!propId) { showToast('Selecciona una propiedad', 'error'); return; }
 820 |   if (!desc)   { showToast('Ingresa la descripción', 'error'); return; }
 821 |   if (!amount || amount <= 0) { showToast('Ingresa un monto válido', 'error'); return; }
 822 |   if (!due)    { showToast('Ingresa la fecha de vencimiento', 'error'); return; }
 823 | 
 824 |   let result;
 825 | 
 826 |   if (unitId) {
 827 |     // Cargo para una sola unidad
 828 |     result = await apiRequest('/charges/', 'POST', {
 829 |       unit_id: unitId, description: desc, amount,
 830 |       date_created: created || todayISO(), due_date: due,
 831 |     });
 832 |   } else {
 833 |     // Cargo general para toda la propiedad
 834 |     result = await apiRequest(`/finance/general-charge/${propId}`, 'POST', {
 835 |       description: desc, amount, due_date: due,
 836 |     });
 837 |   }
 838 | 
 839 |   if (result) {
 840 |     showToast(unitId
 841 |       ? 'Cargo creado correctamente'
 842 |       : `Cargos creados para todas las unidades`);
 843 |     document.getElementById('charge-desc').value   = '';
 844 |     document.getElementById('charge-amount').value = '';
 845 |     document.getElementById('charge-due').value    = '';
 846 |     document.getElementById('amount-preview').textContent = '0.00';
 847 |     await loadChargesTable();
 848 |   }
 849 | }
 850 | 
 851 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 852 | // TABLA HISTORIAL
 853 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 854 | async function loadChargesTable() {
 855 |   allChargesCache = await apiRequest('/finance/charges') || [];
 856 | 
 857 |   // Llenar selects de filtro con valores únicos
 858 |   const owners = [...new Set(allChargesCache.map(c => c.owner_name).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 859 |   const units  = [...new Set(allChargesCache.map(c => c.unit_number).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 860 | 
 861 |   const ownerSel = document.getElementById('filter-owner');
 862 |   const unitSel  = document.getElementById('filter-unit');
 863 | 
 864 |   if (ownerSel) {
 865 |     const prev = ownerSel.value;
 866 |     ownerSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 867 |     owners.forEach(o => ownerSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o}">${o}</option>`);
 868 |     ownerSel.value = prev;
 869 |   }
 870 |   if (unitSel) {
 871 |     const prev = unitSel.value;
 872 |     unitSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 873 |     units.forEach(u => unitSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u}">Apt. ${u}</option>`);
 874 |     unitSel.value = prev;
 875 |   }
 876 | 
 877 |   filterChargesTable();
 878 | }
 879 | 
 880 | function clearChargeFilters() {
 881 |   ['filter-status','filter-owner','filter-unit'].forEach(id => {
 882 |     const el = document.getElementById(id);
 883 |     if (el) el.value = '';
 884 |   });
 885 |   const descEl = document.getElementById('filter-desc');
 886 |   if (descEl) descEl.value = '';
 887 |   filterChargesTable();
 888 | }
 889 | 
 890 | function filterChargesTable() {
 891 |   const status = document.getElementById('filter-status')?.value  || '';
 892 |   const owner  = document.getElementById('filter-owner')?.value   || '';
 893 |   const unit   = document.getElementById('filter-unit')?.value    || '';
 894 |   const desc   = (document.getElementById('filter-desc')?.value   || '').toLowerCase().trim();
 895 | 
 896 |   const list = allChargesCache.filter(c => {
 897 |     if (status && c.status     !== status)                       return false;
 898 |     if (owner  && c.owner_name !== owner)                        return false;
 899 |     if (unit   && c.unit_number!== unit)                         return false;
 900 |     if (desc   && !c.description?.toLowerCase().includes(desc))  return false;
 901 |     return true;
 902 |   });
 903 | 
 904 |   // Actualizar badge
 905 |   const badge = document.getElementById('charges-count-badge');
 906 |   if (badge) badge.textContent = list.length;
 907 | 
 908 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('charges-table-body');
 909 | 
 910 |   if (!list.length) {
 911 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 912 |       Sin cargos con los filtros aplicados</td></tr>`;
 913 |     return;
 914 |   }
 915 | 
 916 |   tbody.innerHTML = list.map(c => {
 917 |     const paid = parseFloat(c.amount || 0) - parseFloat(c.balance || 0);
 918 |     return `<tr>
 919 |       <td>${c.owner_name || '<em style="color:var(--text-muted)">Sin asignar</em>'}</td>
 920 |       <td>${c.unit_number ? `Apt. ${c.unit_number}` : '—'}</td>
 921 |       <td><strong>${c.description}</strong></td>
 922 |       <td style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--text-secondary);">${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 923 |       <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.amount)}</td>
 924 |       <td class="td-right" style="color:var(--success);">$${formatMoney(paid)}</td>
 925 |       <td class="td-right td-bold">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</td>
 926 |       <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 927 |     </tr>`;
 928 |   }).join('');
 929 | }
 930 | renderSidebar('finances');
 931 | init();
 932 | </script>
 933 | </body>
 934 | </html>
 935 |

 179 |         <button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="abrirReporte()" style="width:auto;margin-top:0;">

 215 |         </div>

 309 | 
 310 | let allPagos  = [];
 311 | let filtrados = [];
 312 | 
 313 | /* ── Tag de concepto ─────────────────────────────────── */
 314 | function razonTag(t) {
 315 |   if (!t || t === '—') return `<span class="razon-tag tag-otros">—</span>`;
 316 |   const l = t.toLowerCase();
 317 |   let c = 'tag-otros';
 318 |   if (l.includes('mantenimiento'))                         c = 'tag-mant';
 319 |   else if (l.includes('gas'))                              c = 'tag-gas';
 320 |   else if (l.includes('ascensor') || l.includes('cuota')) c = 'tag-asc';
 321 |   else if (l.includes('admin'))                            c = 'tag-admin';
 322 |   return `<span class="razon-tag ${c}">${t}</span>`;
 323 | }
 324 | 
 325 | /* ── Init ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */
 326 | async function init() {
 327 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('hist-tbody');
 328 |   const pagos = await apiRequest('/finance/payments-history');
 329 | 
 330 |   if (!pagos) {
 331 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--danger);">Error al cargar el historial.</td></tr>`;
 332 |     return;
 333 |   }
 334 |   if (!pagos.length) {
 335 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 336 |       <i class="fas fa-inbox" style="font-size:2rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 337 |       No hay pagos registrados.<br><small>Usa el importador de historial para cargar registros.</small>
 338 |     </td></tr>`;
 339 |     return;
 340 |   }
 341 | 
 342 |   allPagos = pagos.map(p => ({
 343 |     payment_id:  p.payment_id,
 344 |     factura:     p.factura     || '—',
 345 |     fecha:       p.fecha       || '',
 346 |     apto:        p.unit_number || '—',
 347 |     owner_name:  p.owner_name  || '—',
 348 |     concepto:    p.concepto    || '—',
 349 |     observacion: p.observacion || '',
 350 |     monto:       parseFloat(p.monto || 0),
 351 |   })).sort((a, b) => b.fecha.localeCompare(a.fecha));
 352 | 
 353 |   llenarFiltros();
 354 |   aplicar();
 355 |   llenarSelectoresReporte();
 356 | }
 357 | 
 358 | /* ── Selects ──────────────────────────────────────────── */
 359 | function llenarFiltros() {
 360 |   const owners    = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.owner_name))].sort();
 361 |   const aptos     = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.apto))].sort();
 362 |   const conceptos = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.concepto))].sort();
 363 |   document.getElementById('f-owner').innerHTML   += owners.map(o    => `<option>${o}</option>`).join('');
 364 |   document.getElementById('f-apto').innerHTML    += aptos.map(a     => `<option>${a}</option>`).join('');
 365 |   document.getElementById('f-concepto').innerHTML+= conceptos.map(c => `<option>${c}</option>`).join('');
 366 | }
 367 | 
 368 | function llenarSelectoresReporte() {
 369 |   const aptos     = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.apto))].sort();
 370 |   const conceptos = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.concepto))].sort();
 371 |   document.getElementById('rep-apto').innerHTML    += aptos.map(a     => `<option>${a}</option>`).join('');
 372 |   document.getElementById('rep-concepto').innerHTML+= conceptos.map(c => `<option>${c}</option>`).join('');
 373 | }
 374 | 
 375 | /* ── Filtros tabla ───────────────────────────────────── */
 376 | function aplicar() {
 377 |   const owner    = document.getElementById('f-owner').value;
 378 |   const apto     = document.getElementById('f-apto').value;
 379 |   const concepto = document.getElementById('f-concepto').value;
 380 |   const desde    = document.getElementById('f-desde').value;
 381 |   const hasta    = document.getElementById('f-hasta').value;
 382 |   const search   = document.getElementById('f-search').value.toLowerCase().trim();
 383 | 
 384 |   filtrados = allPagos.filter(p => {
 385 |     if (owner    && p.owner_name !== owner)    return false;
 386 |     if (apto     && p.apto       !== apto)     return false;
 387 |     if (concepto && p.concepto   !== concepto) return false;
 388 |     if (desde    && p.fecha < desde)           return false;
 389 |     if (hasta    && p.fecha > hasta)           return false;
 390 |     if (search) {
 391 |       const txt = [p.factura, String(p.monto), p.concepto, p.owner_name, p.apto].join(' ').toLowerCase();
 392 |       if (!txt.includes(search)) return false;
 393 |     }
 394 |     return true;
 395 |   });
 396 |   renderTabla();
 397 |   renderResumen();
 398 | }
 399 | 
 400 | function limpiarFiltros() {
 401 |   ['f-owner','f-apto','f-concepto','f-desde','f-hasta','f-search'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 402 |   aplicar();
 403 | }
 404 | 
 405 | /* ── Tabla ───────────────────────────────────────────── */
 406 | function renderTabla() {
 407 |   document.getElementById('total-count').textContent = filtrados.length;
 408 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('hist-tbody');
 409 |   if (!filtrados.length) {
 410 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 411 |     document.getElementById('page-info').textContent = '';
 412 |     return;
 413 |   }
 414 |   const visible = filtrados.slice(0, 500);
 415 |   tbody.innerHTML = visible.map(p => `
 416 |     <tr>
 417 |       <td class="td-mono" style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">${p.factura}</td>
 418 |       <td style="white-space:nowrap;">${formatDate(p.fecha)}</td>
 419 |       <td><strong>Apt. ${p.apto}</strong></td>
 420 |       <td style="font-size:.83rem;">${p.owner_name}</td>
 421 |       <td>${razonTag(p.concepto)}</td>
 422 |       <td class="td-right"><strong>$${formatMoney(p.monto)}</strong></td>
 423 |     </tr>`).join('');
 424 |   document.getElementById('page-info').textContent =
 425 |     filtrados.length > 500
 426 |       ? `Mostrando 500 de ${filtrados.length} — exporta Excel para ver todos`
 427 |       : `${filtrados.length} registro${filtrados.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
 428 | }
 429 | 
 430 | /* ── Resumen chips ───────────────────────────────────── */
 431 | function renderResumen() {
 432 |   const chips = document.getElementById('summary-chips');
 433 |   if (!filtrados.length) { chips.innerHTML = ''; return; }
 434 |   const total = filtrados.reduce((s, p) => s + p.monto, 0);
 435 |   const porC  = {};
 436 |   filtrados.forEach(p => { porC[p.concepto] = (porC[p.concepto] || 0) + p.monto; });
 437 |   let html = `
 438 |     <div class="s-chip"><strong>${filtrados.length}</strong><span>Registros</span></div>
 439 |     <div class="s-chip"><strong>$${formatMoney(total)}</strong><span>Total</span></div>`;
 440 |   Object.entries(porC).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,5).forEach(([k,v]) => {
 441 |     html += `<div class="s-chip"><strong>$${formatMoney(v)}</strong><span>${k}</span></div>`;
 442 |   });
 443 |   chips.innerHTML = html;
 444 | }
 445 | 
 446 | /* ── Excel general ───────────────────────────────────── */
 447 | function exportarExcel() {
 448 |   if (!filtrados.length) { showToast('Sin datos para exportar','warning'); return; }
 449 |   const headers = ['# Factura','Fecha','Apartamento','Propietario','Concepto','Monto'];
 450 |   const rows    = filtrados.map(p => [p.factura, p.fecha, p.apto, p.owner_name, p.concepto, p.monto]);
 451 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, ...rows]);
 452 |   ws['!cols'] = [{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:28},{wch:22},{wch:12}];
 453 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 454 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, 'Historial');
 455 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, `historial_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`);
 456 |   showToast('Archivo descargado','success');
 457 | }
 458 | 
 459 | /* ══ REPORTE PDF ═══════════════════════════════════════ */
 460 | function abrirReporte() {
 461 |   document.getElementById('reporte-modal').classList.add('open');
 462 | }
 463 | function cerrarReporte() {
 464 |   document.getElementById('reporte-modal').classList.remove('open');
 465 | }
 466 | document.getElementById('reporte-modal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
 467 |   if (e.target === this) cerrarReporte();
 468 | });
 469 | 
 470 | function getPagosFiltradosReporte() {
 471 |   const apto     = document.getElementById('rep-apto').value;
 472 |   const desde    = document.getElementById('rep-desde').value;
 473 |   const hasta    = document.getElementById('rep-hasta').value;
 474 |   const concepto = document.getElementById('rep-concepto').value;
 475 |   if (!apto) return null;
 476 |   let p = allPagos.filter(x => x.apto === apto);
 477 |   if (desde)    p = p.filter(x => x.fecha >= desde);
 478 |   if (hasta)    p = p.filter(x => x.fecha <= hasta);
 479 |   if (concepto) p = p.filter(x => x.concepto === concepto);
 480 |   return { apto, desde, hasta, concepto, pagos: p };
 481 | }
 482 | 
 483 | function fdate(s) {
 484 |   if (!s) return '—';
 485 |   try {
 486 |     const [y,m,d] = s.split('T')[0].split('-');
 487 |     const months = ['ene','feb','mar','abr','may','jun','jul','ago','sep','oct','nov','dic'];
 488 |     return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;
 489 |   } catch { return s; }
 490 | }
 491 | 
 492 | function generarReporte() {
 493 |   const content = document.getElementById('reporte-content');
 494 |   const res = getPagosFiltradosReporte();
 495 | 
 496 |   if (!res) {
 497 |     content.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 498 |       <i class="fas fa-home" style="font-size:2rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 499 |       Selecciona un apartamento para generar el reporte</div>`;
 500 |     return;
 501 |   }
 502 | 
 503 |   const { apto, desde, hasta, concepto, pagos } = res;
 504 | 
 505 |   if (!pagos.length) {
 506 |     content.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin pagos con los filtros seleccionados</div>`;
 507 |     return;
 508 |   }
 509 | 
 510 |   const owner  = pagos[0]?.owner_name || '—';
 511 |   const total  = pagos.reduce((s, p) => s + p.monto, 0);
 512 |   const hoy    = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', { year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' });
 513 |   const periodo= desde && hasta ? `${fdate(desde)} al ${fdate(hasta)}`
 514 |                : desde ? `Desde ${fdate(desde)}`
 515 |                : hasta ? `Hasta ${fdate(hasta)}` : 'Histórico completo';
 516 | 
 517 |   // Resumen por concepto
 518 |   const porC = {};
 519 |   pagos.forEach(p => { porC[p.concepto] = (porC[p.concepto] || 0) + p.monto; });
 520 | 
 521 |   // Intentar logo
 522 |   const logoHtml = `<div class="brand-logo" id="pdf-logo-box">AR</div>`;
 523 | 
 524 |   content.innerHTML = `
 525 |     <div id="pdf-doc" class="pdf-doc">
 526 | 
 527 |       <!-- Cabecera igual al estado de cuenta -->
 528 |       <div class="doc-head">
 529 |         <div class="brand">
 530 |           ${logoHtml}
 531 |           <div class="brand-name">
 532 |             <h1>ALIANZA RESIDENCIAL</h1>
 533 |             <p>Administración de Propiedades</p>
 534 |           </div>
 535 |         </div>
 536 |         <div class="doc-title">
 537 |           <h2>Reporte de Pagos</h2>
 538 |           <p>Generado el ${hoy}</p>
 539 |         </div>
 540 |       </div>
 541 | 
 542 |       <!-- Info del apartamento -->
 543 |       <div class="info-grid">
 544 |         <div class="info-cell">
 545 |           <div class="ic-lbl">Apartamento</div>
 546 |           <div class="ic-val">Apt. ${apto}</div>
 547 |         </div>
 548 |         <div class="info-cell">
 549 |           <div class="ic-lbl">Propietario</div>
 550 |           <div class="ic-val">${owner}</div>
 551 |         </div>
 552 |         <div class="info-cell">
 553 |           <div class="ic-lbl">Período</div>
 554 |           <div class="ic-val" style="font-size:.82rem;">${periodo}</div>
 555 |         </div>
 556 |       </div>
 557 | 
 558 |       <!-- Resumen por concepto -->
 559 |       <div class="section-title">Resumen por concepto</div>
 560 |       <div class="sum-row">
 561 |         ${Object.entries(porC).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).map(([k,v]) => `
 562 |           <div class="sum-chip">
 563 |             <strong>$${formatMoney(v)}</strong>
 564 |             <span>${k}</span>
 565 |           </div>`).join('')}
 566 |       </div>
 567 | 
 568 |       <!-- Tabla de pagos -->
 569 |       <div class="section-title">Detalle de pagos</div>
 570 |       <table>
 571 |         <thead>
 572 |           <tr>
 573 |             <th># Factura</th>
 574 |             <th>Fecha</th>
 575 |             <th>Concepto</th>
 576 |             <th class="r">Monto</th>
 577 |           </tr>
 578 |         </thead>
 579 |         <tbody>
 580 |           ${pagos.map(p => `
 581 |             <tr>
 582 |               <td class="muted">${p.factura}</td>
 583 |               <td>${fdate(p.fecha)}</td>
 584 |               <td>${p.concepto}</td>
 585 |               <td class="r">$${formatMoney(p.monto)}</td>
 586 |             </tr>`).join('')}
 587 |         </tbody>
 588 |       </table>
 589 | 
 590 |       <!-- Totales -->
 591 |       <div class="total-line">
 592 |         <div>
 593 |           <div class="tl">Registros</div>
 594 |           <div class="tv">${pagos.length}</div>
 595 |         </div>
 596 |         <div>
 597 |           <div class="tl">Total pagado</div>
 598 |           <div class="tv">$${formatMoney(total)}</div>
 599 |         </div>
 600 |       </div>
 601 | 
 602 |       <!-- Aviso legal -->
 603 |       <div class="legal-notice">
 604 |         <p>
 605 |           <strong>DOCUMENTO NO FISCAL —</strong>
 606 |           Este reporte es un documento informativo generado por el sistema de administración
 607 |           de Alianza Residencial y <strong>no constituye una factura fiscal ni comprobante de
 608 |           pago con validez tributaria</strong> ante la Dirección General de Ingresos (DGI) u
 609 |           otra autoridad competente. Para efectos fiscales y legales, solicite el recibo o
 610 |           factura oficial emitido al momento del pago.
 611 |         </p>
 612 |       </div>
 613 | 
 614 |       <!-- Footer -->
 615 |       <div class="doc-footer">
 616 |         <div class="doc-footer-left">
 617 |           Alianza Residencial &bull; Sistema de Administración de Propiedades<br>
 618 |           Generado el ${hoy}
 619 |         </div>
 620 |         <div class="firma-line">Firma Administración</div>
 621 |       </div>
 622 | 
 623 |     </div>`;
 624 | 
 625 |   // Cargar logo si existe
 626 |   const logoImg = new Image();
 627 |   logoImg.onload = () => {
 628 |     const box = document.getElementById('pdf-logo-box');
 629 |     if (box) box.innerHTML = `<img src="/static/logo.png" alt="Logo">`;
 630 |   };
 631 |   logoImg.src = '/static/logo.png';
 632 | }
 633 | 
 634 | /* ── Imprimir / Exportar PDF ─────────────────────────── */
 635 | function imprimirPDF() {
 636 |   const apto = document.getElementById('rep-apto').value;
 637 |   if (!apto) { showToast('Selecciona un apartamento primero','warning'); return; }
 638 |   const doc = document.getElementById('pdf-doc');
 639 |   if (!doc)  { showToast('Genera el reporte primero','warning'); return; }
 640 |   window.print();
 641 | }
 642 | 
 643 | /* ── Excel del reporte ───────────────────────────────── */
 644 | function exportarReporteExcel() {
 645 |   const res = getPagosFiltradosReporte();
 646 |   if (!res) { showToast('Selecciona un apartamento primero','warning'); return; }
 647 |   const { apto, pagos } = res;
 648 |   if (!pagos.length) { showToast('Sin datos para exportar','warning'); return; }
 649 | 
 650 |   const total   = pagos.reduce((s,p) => s+p.monto, 0);
 651 |   const headers = ['# Factura','Fecha','Apartamento','Propietario','Concepto','Monto'];
 652 |   const rows    = pagos.map(p => [p.factura, p.fecha, p.apto, p.owner_name, p.concepto, p.monto]);
 653 |   rows.push([], ['','','','','TOTAL', total]);
 654 | 
 655 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, ...rows]);
 656 |   ws['!cols'] = [{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:28},{wch:22},{wch:12}];
 657 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 658 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, `Apt ${apto}`);
 659 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, `reporte_apt${apto}_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`);
 660 |   showToast('Reporte descargado','success');
 661 | }
 662 | 
 663 | init();
 664 | </script>
 665 | </body>
